更新

另请参阅:主页,发展计划和移动更新


下面列出的所有信息也可以在更新说明部分和新闻存档部分.

2026

3月6日（更新823）

更改列表：

  • The 训练场地图已经更新并添加到匹配
    • （注意）该地图支持12名玩家以及除突袭和团队剑圣/JGR之外的所有模式。
  • 增加了负货币支持机制
    • 当支付在游戏外被取消时，该机制会被触发。
    • 支持坦克币、红宝石、水晶以及所有钥匙的负余额。
    • 禁止玩游戏的能力、完成任务、使用一些社交功能，以及访问商店和车库的折扣。
    • （注意）现在，在支付撤销的活动中，账号不会立即被封锁。相反，将对某些功能施加限制，包括游戏功能。要退出此状态，必须偿还因支付撤销而产生的债务。此机制只能使用一次。如果再次出现负余额，账号将像以前一样被封锁。
  • 游戏的Unity版本变更
    • 商店已更新，现在完全类似于 HTML5 版本。
    • 一个由左侧游戏手柄摇杆控制的虚拟光标已被添加到游戏大厅中。
      • （注意）此光标不会取代大厅中的箭头导航，而是对其的补充。
    • 添加了客户端信息行的显示，如同在HTML5中，包括当前服务器编号。
    • 现在，当按住按钮时，战斗玩家表（TAB）会显示，但如果快速按一下，它会保持在屏幕上，直到再次按下按钮。
    • 增加了在 TAB 表中选择单个玩家以发送投诉的功能。
  • 特斯拉
    • 装填时间从1秒减少到0.8秒。
    • 普通伤害从450-900减少到300-400；
    • 为链条中的每个目标增加了300-400 HP的额外伤害提升；
    • (注意) 特斯拉炮塔伤害现在分为两部分。标准伤害按链条中目标的数量照常分配。额外伤害永远不按链条中目标的数量分配。每个目标最终收到的伤害是标准伤害和额外伤害的总和。换句话说，当用链式闪电攻击两个目标时，伤害现在只减少四分之一，而不是减少一半。
  • 极速炮
    • 炮管停止时间从2.5秒减少到1秒。
    • ‘更快速的水平跟踪” 装备改造
      • 减少时间的桶停止效果从 -60% 改为 -50%；
  • 轰天炮
    • 在移动版本中，炮塔现在有一个按钮可以启用/禁用强制射击，类似于离子炮。
  • 蝎子
    • 重新装填时间从 3.9-2.6 秒增加到 4.05-2.7 秒。
    • “真空壳”装备改造
      • 火龙珠已被禁用；
  • 马格南
    • 铁塔的抛射物角度从2度降低到1.5度；
    • 初始弹丸速度从30米/秒降至20米/秒；
    • 最终弹丸速度从120降至110米/秒；
  • 镭射炮
    • 街机射击之间的装填时间从2.25-1.5秒增加到2.7-1.8秒。
    • “短波发射器” 装备改造
      • 街机重装增益从 +34% 改为 +15%；
    • “类星体” 装备改造
      • 街机射击炮弹重装时间增益从 +100% 改为 +70%；
  • 添加了在匹配中禁用不同平台之间跨平台游戏的支持
    • （注意）此功能尚未公开可用。
  • 在屏幕右下角添加了当前服务器编号的显示。

修复列表：

  • Medic 手榴弹现在可以在其效果范围内逐秒恢复坦克血量，而不仅仅是在爆炸瞬间一次性恢复。
    • （注意）预计在三月随着新活动的出现，手榴弹将出现在抢先体验中。
  • 团结
    • 优化后的着色器大小。
    • 已移除适用于1920像素及以上分辨率的小布局。
    • 修复了最近添加到游戏中的新皮肤的外观。
    • 修复了发现的各种小错误。


2月19日（更新822）

更改列表：

  • 向所有标准（非重制）地图添加了雾
    • （注意）重制地图上的雾在此之前就已经可以使用，其具有自己的距离和强度设置。
    • （注意）我们提醒你，雾可以在游戏设置中关闭

    • 圣骑士
      • 0,278% → 0,256% 或 360 → 390 秒用于完整过速装置充能
    • 独裁者
      • 0,476% → 0,333% 或 210 → 300 秒用于完整过速装置充能
    • 泰坦
      • 0,416% → 0,333% 或 240 → 300 秒用于完整过速装置充能
    • 阿瑞斯
      • 0,278% → 0,256% 或 360 → 390 秒用于完整过速装置充能
    • 猛犸象
      • 0,370% → 0,300% 或 270 → 330 秒用于完整过速装置充能
  • 剑圣
    • 过速装置的激活延迟从2秒减少到1.1秒

修复列表：

  • “爆破炮弹”装备改造（用于轰天炮）和“Explosive Shells”装备改造（用于蝎子）的图标已更新，以避免与“真空 Shells”装备改造图标相交

    • 独裁者
      • 0,300% → 0,476% 或 330 → 210 秒用于完全过速装置充能

2025

12月19日（更新818）

更改列表：

  • 对在战斗中发送指令频率超过合理限制的玩家进行了强制断开连接
  • 修正了游戏中的一些文本

修复列表：

  • 修复了火箭炮 DK 皮肤上射击准备指示器的问题
  • 修复了高清皮肤的动态细节工作
  • 修复了特斯拉效果导致内存泄漏的问题
  • 修复了商店中支付方式的排序
  • 《边塞角斗场》和《高原 Remastered》地图的优化
  • 旧新年地图现在已被 Unity 客户端支持

    • (注意) 您需要有效的VIP通行证才能完成这些任务，就像完成此类每周任务一样
  • “礼炮” 手榴弹
    • “礼炮”手榴弹发射器可以在商店以183,000水晶购买，起始等级为中将（25）
    • “礼炮”手榴弹可以在商店以1800水晶购买
    • 手榴弹可以作为“抢先体验物品”的一部分在商店购买
    • “眩晕”效果持续时间从3秒减少到2.5秒。
  • 现在如果你尝试在你的队伍中有超过2名玩家时寻找战斗，你的队伍将被自动解散
    • (注意) 我们发现，由于集群中游戏服务器的同步特性，在罕见情况下有可能随机创建一个包含超过2名玩家的小组。现在，这样的小组将会被自动解散，小组中的所有玩家将分别进入战斗。如果你的小组中误加入了超过2名玩家，请将多余的玩家移出小组，这样你们两名玩家就可以一起游戏。
  • 在商店的每日红宝石通行证类别中添加了一个计时器，显示当前红宝石通行证优惠结束的时间

  • 修复了 Safari 中的鼠标捕获问题，释放 TAB 后导致的焦点丢失

7月25日（更新806）

更改列表：

  • 以下装备改造已添加到普通和史诗幸运礼盒中
    • 火箭炮的“露营者”
    • 阿瑞斯’ “榴弹兵”
  • 最高小组大小从3减至2玩家
    • （注意）在分析了关于匹配中小组平衡问题的反馈后，我们观察到玩家行为发生了显著变化。现在，两名玩家的小组数量远远超过三名玩家的小组。与此同时，玩家认为三名玩家的小组本质上比两名玩家的小组更强。我们认为这种组合导致了团队平衡的不稳定。鉴于对两名玩家小组的需求远高于三名玩家小组，我们已决定禁用创建三名玩家小组的选项。
  • 小组成员之间允许的等级差从5增加到20
    • （注意）此更改与之前的更改有关。两个玩家小组中的等级差距比三个玩家小组中的等级差距引起的匹配问题更少。鉴于两个玩家小组的高度兴趣，我们希望鼓励更多的双人游戏。我们希望不会后悔这个决定。我们将监控情况并关注您的反馈。
  • 当没有其他活跃活动模式时，死亡混战模式默认作为一个活动模式启用。
    • 这个模式从二级军士长（8）开始开放，就像其他活动模式一样
    • 此模式的地图池包括所有匹配地图和Pro地图
    • 战斗奖励、经验值获取和金箱子不会增加
  • 轰天炮
    • 暴击几率从14%降低到13%

    • （注意）因此，在升级火焰炮或冰风暴的 Mk1 改造后，它不会在整整一秒内提高能量充能速度

3月28日（更新794）

更改列表：

  • 实现了贴花（爆炸痕迹）的阴影和光照效果。
    • （注意）目前仅支持阴影贴图；光照贴图将在重制的地图中于未来世界中支持。
  • 当地雷被放置时，3D模型上会出现白色闪光效果，就像在Flash客户端中一样。
  • 战斗中某些行为获得的经验值减少了25%（40经验值 → 30经验值，20经验值 → 15经验值）。
      • 我们在之前的视频日志中宣布了这一变化，当时我们提到2020年的经验值获取速度增加了四倍。在此变化之后，与2020年相比，经验值获取速度将从x4下降到x3。战斗中获得的奖励将保持在2020年的x2等级。在分析这一变化的结果后，我们将决定是否有必要将经验值获取速度从x3减少到x2。
  • The 金箱子现在提供经验值
      • 标准金箱子 — +1000 经验值
      • 幸运礼盒箱子 — +1000 经验值
      • Megagold with 水晶 — +5000 经验值
      • Megagold with 红宝石 — +1000 经验值
      • Custom 金箱子 — +0 经验值
      • 坦克爆炸在愚人节金箱子 — +0 经验值
  • 标准每日和每周任务现在包括完成每个任务可获得+100经验值作为奖励。
  • 完成每日超级任务获得的红宝石数量从3个减少到2个。
  • 完成每周超级任务的红宝石数量从5增加到12。
  • 肾上腺素装备改造的机制已被更改。现在，这些装备改造仅在坦克的生命值降至某个阈值以下时提供额外伤害。伤害不再随着坦克生命值的下降而线性增加。
    • 近战炮塔（火焰炮、冰风暴、磁力炮、特斯拉、滑膛炮）
    • 额外25%的伤害
      • 当生命值降至35%时，触发奖励激活。
    • 中等射程炮塔（离子炮、火龙珠、极速炮、轰天炮、火箭炮、雷暴炮）
    • 额外 25% 伤害
      • 当生命值降至25%时，触发奖励激活。
    • 长射程炮塔（蝎子、马格南、激光炮、电磁炮、镭射炮）
      • 额外 25% 伤害
      • 当生命值降至20%时，触发奖励激活。
  • “Complete 每日任务” 每周任务的要求已从35改为15。
  • 《在战斗中获取声望点》的每周任务要求已从3000更改为4000。
  • «Earn 水晶 in 战斗» 每周任务的要求从2000变更为7000。
  • «在战斗中获得经验值» 每周任务的要求已从4000更改为5000。
  • «道具 Pack» 特殊优惠现在花费 500 红宝石，而不是 500 坦克币。
  • 添加了«Starter Key 礼包»特殊优惠，其中包括45个普通钥匙，享受90%的折扣。
  • 新增了«传奇 Key 礼包»特殊优惠，其中包括5个传奇钥匙，享受90%的折扣。
  • «炸弹»手榴弹（所有改装）已加入抢先体验套件
  • «迫击炮» 手榴弹（Mk1 改进型）已添加到抢先体验套件中

修复列表：

  • 修复了Unity客户端在Nintendo Switch上有时无法通过数据*处理协议屏幕的一个错误。
  • 现在，当阴影开启时，场景中主方向光的强度不会减弱；画面不会变暗。
  • 在战斗中更换装备时，已移除在看不见的大厅中不必要的坦克重新组装。
  • 在车库中禁用了底盘轨迹的阴影。
  • 战斗中用于缓存奖励箱的系统已经得到了改进。
  • 修复了一个错误，该错误导致商店中展示类别的商店优惠在升级后未被发放。

12月6日（更新785）

List of changes:

  • Changed how ricocheting works. Now, after a projectile 火龙珠, its 速度 is equal to the initial 速度, no matter what its 速度 was before ricocheting.
  • （注意）这种行为适用于所有拥有可以发射火龙珠的弹丸并且具有不同初始和最终弹丸速度的炮塔
  • 火龙珠
    • Initial projectile 速度 remains 90-180
    • 最终弹丸速度从 90-180 降低到 10-10
    • Time to reach final projectile 速度 increased from 0 to 1
    • “等离子体共振器” 装备改造:
      • 投射物速度增加已从 +50% 改为 +0%。
  • 轰天炮
    • 初始投射物速度保持在400-700
    • 最终弹丸速度从400-700降至300-500
    • Time to reach final projectile 速度 increased from 0 to 0.5
  • 极速炮
    • Initial projectile 速度 increased from 200-250 to 200-300
    • Final projectile 速度 decreased from 200-250 to 100-100
    • Time to reach final projectile 速度 increased from 0 to 0.5
  • 蝎子
    • Initial projectile 速度 remains 500-1000
    • Final projectile 速度 decreased from 500-1000 to 250-500
    • Time to reach final projectile 速度 increased from 0 to 0.5
  • The number of 地雷 in the 战斗 is limited to 10 000. In case this number is reached, it will not be possible to put any more 地雷. The button for placing the 地雷 will be inactivated.
    • (Note) This is a necessary addition in order to increase the stability of 服务器 and to get rid of accompanying errors.

November 14th (Update 782)

List of changes:

  • Added a setting that disables 游戏手柄 configuration by default
    • (Note) Disabling this setting does not turn off 游戏手柄 support completely, but 允许 you to set a custom 控制 layout through third-party applications.
  • 坦克 with a «fixed» 炮塔 (马格南, B0-NK) with the select «鼠标 + 键盘» 控制模式 can no longer switch to 键盘控制模式 without entering the game 设置.
    • (Note) This is necessary in order to be able to lower and raise the barrel while holding down the 射击 button. Previously, when trying to change the shot angle, the game switched to 键盘控制模式 and shot automatically.
  • The VFX 道具 activation effect for «速度提升» is now linked to different points for different 底盘, and hover 坦克 have one trail on the ground instead of two
  • The VFX 道具 activation effect for «护甲提升» was slightly sped up to better match the animation 速度 of the «伤害提升» and «速度提升» VFX effects.

List of fixes:

  • Fixed the switch to 键盘控制. Now it works only by pressing «C» (炮塔 centering).
    • (Note) Previously, you could switch by pressing Z/X, and this created problems in some cases.
  • Fixed dead 动感区域 for 控制 sticks in the mobile version
    • (Note) This behavior was intended only for 游戏手柄.
  • Reduced the angle at which a hover 底盘 stops turning to the direction of the 炮塔
    • (Note) This will 允许 for more precise hover rotation, which will be very useful for 十字军, for example
  • Fixed displaying the self-destruct launch progress bar when holding the button after self-destruction has already been launched.

  • Added a new 马格南装备改造 to 史诗幸运礼盒 - «破坏者»
    • (Note) 普通 and 暴击伤害 are increased. Impact, explosion force, and 后坐力 force are also increased. Reload takes longer. 炮塔 rotation 速度, projectile 速度, and explosion 半径 are decreased.
  • Added experimental 游戏手柄 support (only in 战斗)

October 25th (Update 779)

List of changes:

  • A new in-game currency, 红宝石, has been added to the game.
    • (Note) All 坦克币 on 玩家' 账号 are saved. 坦克币 may be exchanged for 红宝石 in a 1:1 ratio through a 特殊 menu with confirmation. You can find out about the 原因 for introducing a new currency in our 视频日志 or in a separate 公告 that has already been published on all our information platforms.
  • 坦克币 are hidden from the main interface and will now only appear in the 商店.
  • The 每日坦克币通行证 has been replaced with 每日红宝石通行证.
    • When you purchase this 通行证, you instantly receive 坦克币, and then 红宝石 will be awarded for the pre-completed 每日任务. The first time you 购买 a 每日坦克币通行证 it will remain unchanged (it will award 坦克币 initially and also for the 每日 pre-completed 任务).
  • VIP 通行证 and some limited 特价优惠 are now sold for 坦克币.
  • 特价优惠 for 活动, 战斗 and 精英通行证, Keys, 水晶, early access offers, 军团许可证, 昵称 changes, Stars, 金箱子 and 活动 currencies (energy) are now sold for 红宝石.
  • Weapon 升级 when lacking 水晶 and the purchase of modifications will now be in 红宝石 instead of 坦克币.
    • (Note) 升级 prices have not changed
  • The 奖励 in 坦克币 is replaced with 红宝石 in all 任务, 幸运礼盒, 未来世界星级挑战 and 兑换码.
    • (Note) In the current 星级挑战, the final prize will remain 坦克币.
  • 迷彩 sold for 坦克币 are now sold for 红宝石
    • (Note) Except for the «坦克币坦克» 迷彩, which will continue to be sold for 坦克币.
  • Added a new variant of the Megagold — 红宝石 Megagold, which will give you 10 红宝石.
    • (Note) The default 水晶 Megagold is not removed and will also drop in 战斗.
  • Unlocking additional 防护模块 slots is now done for 水晶 instead of 坦克币
    • (Note) Unlocks will cost 5,000, 50,000, and 500,000 水晶 respectively.
  • A new type of 手榴弹 has been added — 南瓜.
    • (Note) This 手榴弹 can only be obtained in the Autumn Mini-game. The 手榴弹 differs from the standard one with modified characteristics and the ability to set enemy 坦克 on fire.
  • «布鲁特斯» 无人机
    • The 最低等级 to purchase it has been changed from 8 to 15
    • This 无人机 can no longer be received from 幸运礼盒
  • Added a VFX effect when activating the «速度提升» 道具 for 危机 and 神谕者无人机.

List of fixes:

  • Fixed a bug that caused the rocket trail effect of the 蝎子 to change its color.
  • In the sniper 模式 of 镭射炮, the «伤害提升» 道具’s effect is no longer displayed if 危机 or 神谕者无人机 is 装备.

    • Mk2: 10 → 5 steps

  • (Note) The total cost of 升级 hasn’t changed, you just need fewer clicks to make at the lower 等级. Existing 升级 steps are automatically converted.
    • 炮塔 and 底盘 are now using .a3d models instead of .3ds to separate the physical and visual parts of the 坦克.
  • (Note) This change should 帮助 reduce frame rate drops when entering 战斗. The old system made the game calculate the physical details on the 玩家’s device, but the new 格式 makes those details ready to go. You'll likely see a big improvement on mobile devices.
  • Bots now support multiple 玩家 in a 战斗 at the same time.
    • (Note) Up to the 等级 of 一级军士长, 玩家 will 战斗 against both 其他玩家 and bots.
  • For 等级 from 一等兵 to 一级军士长, the 匹配 system now add bots instead of increasing the 射程 of 等级.
    • (Note) Empty spots in these 战斗 will now be filled by bots.
  • 冰风暴
    • «肾上腺素» 装备改造

普通 and 暴击伤害 increase changed from +23% to +20%;

  • 离子炮
    • «等离子体涡轮加速器» 装备改造
      • 普通伤害 decrease changed from -45% to -50%;
  • 模块
    • 最低等级 required to purchase the «蜘蛛» 防护模块 increased from 二等兵 (2) to 军士长 (10)
  • 团队剑圣 and JGR 模式 are no longer available for the Siege 匹配地图
  • Changed bases and respawns in the 突袭模式 for the «2042» 地图
  • Changed geometry of the «2042» 地图

The list of fixes:

  • Fixed the bug that caused creating 军团 be available even before a 玩家 reaches the 等级 that unlocks access to the 军团 system

July 12th (Update 767)

List of changes:

  • Bots are now able to function with several real 玩家 in the 战斗 at the same time.
  • 匹配战斗 from the 等级 of X1 to X2 now prioritize the reduction of 玩家 count rather than increasing the 等级 distribution.
    • (Note) 免费 places in such 战斗 will be filled with bots.
  • Added temporary contracts for the new mini-game.
    • (Note) All contracts received at the time of the 活动 will stop being valid after the 活动 ends.
  • Added a category to the 商店 where you can 购买 Contracts.
    • (Note) The new category will stay in the game until the end of the mini-game.
  • Added an experimental feature to 设置 allowing to disable system mouse acceleration.
    • (Note) It will be useful for those who 经验值 sudden 镜头移动 when turning. The 镜头灵敏度 will have to be changed each time you change this setting.
  • Now spending 坦克币 on upgrading the 装备 modification will increase the parameters just like a 普通 modification 升级.
    • (Note) The current parameters of your 装备 may be changed to 账号 for the update, but the current 升级等级 of your 装备 will stay the same.
  • Added an option to the 暂停 menu to 刷新 the game window.
    • (Note) When encountering errors, you will now be able to 刷新 the game without having to relaunch the whole client.

List of fixes:

  • Improved the 后坐力 of 十字军’s 过速装置 shot.
  • 马格南’s “鱼叉导弹” 装备改造 added to 普通 and 史诗幸运礼盒.

May 17th (Update 763)

  • Updated the 声音 of the 激光炮’s «Magic» 射击效果
  • The logic of the 工兵装备改造 has been changed for all 底盘.
    • Instead of a fixed number of protected 地雷, the 装备改造 now retains only 70% of the 地雷 placed after each respawn of the 坦克 with 工兵.
    • The saved 地雷 are chosen randomly
    • (Note) The previous mechanic allowed 地雷 to be placed much more frequently by self-destructing the 坦克 after each 地雷 placement. The new mechanic not only prevents accelerated mining, but also adds counterplay. Now, attackers have the option of accelerating demining by destroying the 工兵, and the 工兵 must remember to protect themselves in order to maintain the 最高 number of 地雷 in defense.

  • The number of 任务 required in the 每周 «Complete 每日任务» 任务 increased from 30 to 35
  • The encore «Successfully deliver 旗子/球 to the correct base» 任务 is removed from the game
  • The 每周 «Earn reputation points in the «团队对战» (团队对战) 模式» 任务 has been replaced with a new «Earn 2000 reputation points by playing in 战斗 you entered via the “Quick 战斗” button» 任务
  • The 每周 «Earn reputation points in the «控制点» (控制点) 模式» 任务 has been replaced with a new «Earn 3000 reputation points in 战斗» 任务
  • The 每周 «Earn reputation points in the «互夺军旗» (互夺军旗) 模式» 任务 has been replaced with a new «Play till the end in 12 战斗» 任务
  • The 每周 «Earn reputation points in the «突袭» (突袭) 模式» 任务 has been replaced with a new «Earn 2000 水晶 in 战斗» 任务
  • The 每周 «Earn reputation points in the «橄榄球» (橄榄球) 模式» 任务 has been replaced with a new «Earn 4000 经验值 in 战斗» 任务
  • The 每周 «Earn reputation points in the «团队剑圣» (团队剑圣) 模式» 任务 has been replaced with a new «Activate 400 of any 道具 in 战斗» 任务
  • The 每周 «Earn reputation points in the «Siege» (围城大战) 模式» 任务 has been replaced with a new «Earn 60 stars» 任务
  • The «Spectrum» 防护模块 now have the default 防护 of 5% and can be upgraded to 15%, 20%, 25% or 30% (depending on a type of a 模块) for a small amount of 水晶
    • (Note) In some 特殊模式升级 are disabled and 普通模块 have 低防护等级 there. As for 玩家 with these 特殊模块, they have an unintended advantage that might seem unfair to 其他玩家. To avoid controversial situations, we changed the initial 防护 value to 5% for all such 模块, and made the total 升级 price 最低, so owners of these 模块 won’t need to spend significant amounts of 水晶. The total price of full 升级 of the Spectrum 模块 will not exceed 15,000 水晶.
  • Removed the option to 报告 messages in 军团聊天
  • Optimised the render system in the HTML5 client


March 7th (Update 755)

  • Added a new 马格南装备改造 to 史诗幸运礼盒 - «眩晕核心».
    • (Note) 暴击伤害 applies the «眩晕» 状态效果 to an enemy 坦克 for a short time.
  • 激光炮射击效果 visual 重制.
    • New effect also applies to all existing 激光炮射击效果.
  • 道具 are now sold in packages with 1, 100, 1000, 3000, and 9999 道具.
    • 金箱子 can now be purchased in 车库, but not in the 商店
  • Reworked the 幸运礼盒 opening mechanic.
    • Fixed the problem with opening 幸运礼盒 on mobile devices.
    • Now when a 幸运礼盒 is opened only the current 奖励 will be shown, and not 奖励 for 幸运礼盒 already opened.
    • Added a new screen after receiving 奖励 one by one that shows all the 奖励.
    • Opening 奖励 one by one can now be skipped.
  • Added a mechanic to 报告 messages in 大厅聊天.
    • Added a button in the context menu that sends an anonymous 报告 that will be seen by the moderators.
  • Added a mechanic to 报告 PRO-战斗 names
    • Added the ability to send an anonymous 报告 that will be seen by the moderators.
  • Added a mechanic to 报告 messages in 战斗聊天.
    • Pressing a 特殊 button right to the 聊天 input or pressing Ctrl + Enter in your 键盘 opens a window with all the messages in the 战斗.
    • Clicking on an individual message in this list will 允许 you to send a 报告 that will be seen by the moderators
  • An experimental 3D indicator of the direction of 伤害 received can be turned on in the game 设置.
    • (Note) We would like to hear your feedback about how this prototype works
  • Fixed the bug that made the interface much bigger than intended on certain phones.

    • 瞄准 time increased from 0.8 to 1 s
    • Reload after 齐射 increased from 0.8-1 to 2.6-1.4 s
    • 暴击伤害几率 increased from 5-15% to 15%
  • 剑圣
    • 防护 decreased from 7 500-30 000 to 5 000-20 000

February 16th (Update 752)

  • Added a new 极速炮装备改造 to 史诗幸运礼盒 — «磁性带».
    • (Note) 暴击伤害 applies the «电磁脉冲» 状态效果 to the enemy 坦克.
  • Changed the way you get stars for 战斗
    • Now the 最高 number of stars you can get per 战斗 depends on 战斗持续时间.
      • (Note) A 战斗 should last at least 11 minutes for the TOP-1 玩家 to get 3 stars. If a 战斗 lasts less than 3 minutes, 玩家 don’t receive stars at all.
    • For 战斗 that are longer than 13 minutes, i.e. 特殊模式战斗, the 最高 number of stars is not limited to 3.
      • (Note) For a 战斗 that lasts 30 minutes, the TOP-1 玩家 may get 8 stars.
  • Entering a 匹配战斗 with the «Quick 战斗» button gives you an extra star.
    • (Note) Thus you may get a total of 4 stars per 战斗, or 8 if you have VIP 通行证.
  • Added a number showing your 几率 to get the item in the list of 幸运礼盒奖励.
    • (Note) 几率 are different for each 玩家 because they depend on how many of the 其他 items available that you already have.
  • Fixed the bug that crashed the game client when you click the 任务 tab once a 战斗 finishes.
  • Fixed the bug that crashed the game client when you redeem certain promocodes.
  • Fixed the bug that caused your 坦克’s 镜头 to stay at the place your 坦克 was destroyed and your 坦克 not respawning.
  • Fixed how the shot geometry works when you use 镭射炮’s 狙击模式.

  • Changed 任务奖励

2023

December 22nd (Update 750)

  • Keys
    • Instead of 普通幸运礼盒, 玩家 now receive 普通 Keys
    • Instead of 每周任务礼盒, 玩家 now receive 珍奇 Keys
    • Instead of 超级礼盒, 玩家 now receive 史诗 Keys
    • Instead of 皮肤礼盒, 玩家 now receive 传奇 Keys
    • (Note) You no longer earn 幸运礼盒. They are now always available in the 幸运礼盒 menu screen. However, you need to earn keys. A key is used to open a 幸运礼盒 of the same type.
  • 玩家 no longer have units of 幸运礼盒 in the 车库
    • If a 玩家 agreed to the conversion procedure, 1 key has been added for each 10 幸运礼盒 they had.
    • If a 玩家 didn’t agree to the conversion procedure, all the 幸运礼盒 in their 车库 have been opened and the prizes added to their 账号.
  • The contents of 史诗幸运礼盒 have been updated.
    • Added a new 装备改造 for 火箭炮 — «真空导弹»
      • (Note) The further a target is from the epicenter of the explosion, the more 伤害 it receives. Pressing the fire button again immediately detonates the missile while it is still in the air.
    • Added the «爆破手» 装备改造 for 黄蜂轻甲, 蜂王, and 霍珀
    • Added the «救生员» 装备改造 for 维京, 十字军, 猎人中甲, 圣骑士, and 独裁者
    • Added the «工兵» 装备改造 for 阿瑞斯, 泰坦, and 猛犸象
  • 史诗 Keys are now always available in the 商店.
  • Added 坦克币 to 每周任务
    • (Note) This is to compensate for the lack of 坦克币 in 珍奇幸运礼盒 which replaced 每周任务礼盒.
  • Improved the captcha feature.

  • Fixed 任务 icons for 每日 and 每周任务
  • Changed the time when in-game 视频日志公告 appear
  • Fixed the bug which caused the 球 drop 动感区域 to be shown wrong
  • Added experimental 选项 to 设置

August 4th (Update 734)

  • Added a new 装备改造 to 超级礼盒 for 磁力炮 — «磁性纳米机器人»
    • (Note) This 装备改造 disables opponents’ 道具 with 暴击 hits.
  • New 格式 for 每日 and 每周任务 has been introduced.
    • 玩家 do not receive three 任务 of each kind anymore
    • 每日任务 can not be changed for 水晶 anymore
    • With the update, all current 每日 and 每周任务 will be removed from the game, whether completed or not.
    • One-time compensation will be issued for the 每周任务 that are not yet completed.
  • 每日任务 have been updated
    • Standard set of 每日任务:
      • Supermission: Complete all the 每日任务. They reset every day.
      • Earn 经验值 in 战斗. (1000 points)
      • Earn reputation points in 战斗. (700 points)
      • Earn 水晶 in 战斗. Only 水晶 visible on the 战斗 end screen are counted. (500 水晶)
      • Earn stars. Both the set of stars you earn in 战斗 and stars you receive for completing 其他任务 are counted. (14 stars)
      • Activate any 道具 in 战斗. Both activating your own set of 道具 and collecting 奖励箱 are counted. (100 道具)
      • Activate 过速装置 in 战斗. (6 过速装置)
      • Play till the end in 匹配战斗. Lack of activity in a 战斗 may prevent the completion of this 任务. (3 战斗)
      • Finish 战斗 by being in the winning 团队. (1 战斗)
      • Make any purchase in the game's 商店. It contains some items that only cost a small amount of 水晶. (1 item)
    • Additional ENCORE set of 每日任务 that become available only after completing the standard set.
      • Supermission: Complete all the additional 每日任务.
      • Destroy enemy 坦克. (15 坦克)
      • Destroy enemy 坦克 with 暴击伤害. When you destroy an enemy with 暴击伤害, their 炮塔 gets blown off the 底盘. (2 坦克)
      • Get into the TOP-3 of your 团队 in 战斗. It doesn't matter if your 团队 is losing. (1 time)
      • Use the «护甲提升» 道具. Both using your own set of 道具 and collecting 奖励箱 are counted. (50 道具)
      • Use the «伤害提升» 道具. Both using your own set of 道具 and collecting 奖励箱 are counted. (50 道具)
      • Use the «速度提升» 道具. Both using your own set of 道具 and collecting 奖励箱 are counted. (50 道具)
      • Open a 普通幸运礼盒 and enjoy the 奖励 for your hard work. (1 幸运礼盒)
    • 每日任务 reset every day, regardless of whether they were completed or not
      • (Note) Do not forget to claim the 奖励 as soon as you complete the 任务.
    • It is enough to complete the 普通 set of 任务 to receive the usual set of prizes in the form of 3 幸运礼盒 and 9 stars
  • 每周任务 have been updated.
    • Standard set of 每周任务:
      • Supermission: Complete all the 每周任务. They reset every week.
      • Complete 每日任务. (30 任务)
      • Finish 战斗 by being in the winning 团队. (4 战斗)
      • Earn reputation points in the «团队对战» (团队对战) 模式. (300 points)
      • Earn reputation points in the «控制点» (控制点) 模式. (300 points)
      • Earn reputation points in the «互夺军旗» (互夺军旗) 模式. (300 points)
      • Earn reputation points in the «突袭» (突袭) 模式. (300 points)
      • Earn reputation points in the «橄榄球» (橄榄球) 模式. (300 points)
      • Earn reputation points in the «团队剑圣» (团队剑圣) 模式. (300 points)
      • Earn reputation points in the «Siege» (围城大战) 模式. (300 points)
    • Additional ENCORE set of 每周任务 that become available only after completing the standard set.
      • Supermission: Complete all the additional 每周任务.
      • Use the «核能» 道具. Both using your own set of 道具 and collecting 奖励箱 are counted. (3 道具)
      • Successfully deliver 旗子/球 to the correct base. You can complete this 任务 in the «互夺军旗», «突袭», and «橄榄球» 模式. (2 times)
      • Capture points. You can complete this 任务 in the «控制点» and «Siege» 模式. (12 points)
      • Destroy a 剑圣. (1 剑圣)
      • Play till the end in 匹配战斗. Lack of activity in a 战斗 may prevent the completion of this 任务. (9 战斗)
      • Finish 战斗 by being in the winning 团队. (3 战斗)
      • Get into the TOP-3 of your 团队 in 战斗. It doesn't matter if your 团队 is losing. (2 times)
    • Additional SECRET set of 每周任务 that becomes available only after completing the additional ENCORE set of 每周任务, and requires VIP 通行证 to claim the prizes:
      • Supermission: Complete all the secret 每周任务. You need to have VIP 通行证 to complete them.
      • Earn 经验值 in 战斗. (1500 points)
      • Earn reputation points in 战斗. (1000 points)
      • Earn 水晶 in 战斗. Only 水晶 visible in the 战斗 end screen are counted. (3000 水晶)
      • Earn stars. Both stars you earned in 战斗 and stars you receive for completing 其他任务 are counted. (15 stars)
      • Use 道具. Both using your own set of 道具 and collecting 奖励箱 are counted. (400 道具)
    • 每周任务 reset every week, regardless of whether they were completed (partially/impartially) or not
      • (Note) Do not forget to claim the 奖励 as soon as you complete the 任务.
    • It is enough to complete the 普通 set of 任务 to receive the usual set of prizes in the form of 9 幸运礼盒, 27 stars and 3 每周任务礼盒.
  • Progress on 每日 and 每周任务 is now displayed on the 战斗 end screen
  • Updated the limits for earning 水晶 and 经验值 in 专家战场
    • Now the limits are updated 每周 instead of being updated 每日
    • Limit of received 水晶 has been changed from 3000-15000 to 21000-105000 水晶
    • Limit of received 经验值 has been changed from 1000-10000 to 7000-70000 points
    • Limit of received 水晶 for VIP 通行证 owners has been changed from 3000-66000 to 21000-462000 水晶
    • Limit of received 经验值 for VIP 通行证 owners has been changed from 1000-22000 to 7000-154000 points
  • 无人机 and 防护模块 are also hidden with a question mark.
  • 装备改造 not owned by the 玩家 are also hidden with a question mark.
  • 底盘 descriptions now contain a video showing its 过速装置 in use.
  • Fixed the description of 电磁炮’ «超高速炮弹» 装备改造
    • (Note) The absence of 伤害 increase for 齐射 shots is not a bug, but a feature.
  • Fixed a bug due to which the 魔术师无人机 did not cause 冷却 of 其他道具.
    • (Note) The absence of 道具冷却 for 魔术师 was a bug, not a feature.
  • Fixed a bug due to which double-clicking did not work to 装备装备改造 or 皮肤
  • Fixed a bug due to which the descriptions of all 装备改造 displayed only half of the description text.
  • Fixed a bug due to which it was impossible to 升级 the 猛犸象底盘.
  • Fixes and improvements to the mobile HTML5 client interface
    • (Note) Optimization and performance improvements of the mobile client will come in next updates


July 28th (Update 733)

  • Fixed bots’ weird behaviour
    • (Note) This bug usually appeared in the 傍晚 and made bots drive backward, not move, not 射击, etc.
  • Added a 特殊 question mark icon for items that are not yet available for new 玩家
    • (Note) It also works for items that have been added to the game but not yet publicly announced
  • 维修工具
    • Delay between repair ticks (actions) increased from 150 to 250 ms
    • The number of HP repaired per tick decreased from 150 to 100 HP
    • The number of repair ticks (actions) increased from 20 to 30
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 30 to 22 s
      • (Note) The frequency of using 维修工具 will remain the same - 30 seconds, despite that reload 持续时间 is increased. It will be so because the increased 道具 effect 持续时间 is 8 seconds and stacks with the 冷却, making it 30 seconds in total
  • 护甲提升
    • Effect 持续时间 increased from 30 to 40 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 20 to 15 s
  • 伤害提升
    • Effect 持续时间 increased from 30 to 40 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 20 to 15 s
  • 速度提升
    • Effect 持续时间 increased from 30 to 40 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 20 to 15 s
  • 地雷
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 3999 to 2000 HP
    • 暴击 hit 几率 increased from 5 to 10%
  • Mechanic
    • Reduction of 维修工具冷却 changed from 15 to 10-20 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 3 to 1 s;
    • Removed the decrease of 炮弹重装时间 of 维修工具道具 by activating 其他道具
  • 守卫者
    • 启动加速度 up 持续时间 changed from 30 to 20-40 s
    • Additional 护甲提升道具启动加速度 increased from 10-90% to 30-90%
    • Reduction of 护甲提升冷却 changed from 5 to 5-15 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 3 to 1 s;
    • Removed the decrease of 炮弹重装时间 of 护甲提升道具 by activating 其他道具
  • 助推器
    • 启动加速度 up 持续时间 changed from 30 to 20-40 s
    • Reduction of 伤害提升冷却 changed from 5 to 5-15 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 3 to 1 s;
    • Removed the decrease of 炮弹重装时间 of 伤害提升道具 by activating 其他道具
  • 魔术师
    • 启动加速度 up 持续时间 changed from 30 to 20-40 s
    • Reduction of 速度提升冷却 changed from 5 to 5-15 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 3 to 1 s;
    • Removed the decrease of 炮弹重装时间 of 速度提升道具 by activating 其他道具
  • 破坏者
    • Reduction of 地雷冷却 0-10 s
    • Reload 持续时间 decreased from 3 to 1 s;
  • 亥伯龙神
    • Reduced 炮弹重装时间 for 道具 changed from 10-20 to 5-15 s
      • (Note) 无人机 behavior doesn't actually change because the 冷却 of main 道具 is reduced from 20 to 15 seconds
  • 危机
    • Reduction of 维修工具 and 地雷冷却 0-5 s
  • 蜘蛛防护模块
    • The 最低等级 required is decreased from 上将 (26) to 新兵 (1)


July 21st (Update 732)

  • Added a new 装备改造 for 电磁炮 to 超级礼盒 — «超高速炮弹»
    • (Note) The shell 伤害 is reduced by 50% at close 射程. The greater the distance, the more 伤害 you deal, allowing you to deliver up to 300% of the 普通 shell 伤害 at the 最高 distance. Shells fly faster, however 暴击伤害 is completely removed.
  • The standard 皮肤 for 电磁炮 has now been updated to an HD version.
    • (Note) 齐射 reloading time is now visually indicated by steam coming out of the 炮塔. The 炮塔 is ready to 射击 again once the steam stops venting.
  • Added new 装备改造 for 电磁炮 that are available for 水晶
    • «更快的水平跟踪» — increases the 炮塔 rotation 速度 and the vertical 瞄准 angle.
    • «入侵瞄准处理器» — significantly increases the time that you stay locked onto the target after it moves out of your sight.
    • «大口径» — increases the 伤害 of standard shots, but the projectiles travel much slower.
  • Updated 皮肤礼盒
    • Added the 冰风暴 XT 皮肤
    • Added the 激光炮 GT 皮肤
    • Amount of 坦克币 obtainable from 皮肤礼盒 has been reduced from 3990 to 1001.
  • Minor text improvements


July 14th (Update 731)

  • A new 装备改造 for 马格南 has been added to 超级礼盒 — «磁性核心»
    • (Note) Every shot applies the «电磁脉冲» 状态效果 to all targets caught in the explosion 半径. With 暴击 hits, the 持续时间 of the effect increases.
  • Bots
    • Bots are added for 等级 starting from 等级 1 (新兵) to 6 (上士)
    • Optimized 服务器 performance of bots
    • Fixed the bug with bots getting progress in 任务 as if they were 玩家
    • For 战斗 with bots, the 战斗持续时间 depends on a 玩家’s 等级
      • 新兵 — 4 minutes
      • 二等兵 — 6 minutes
      • 下士 — 8 minutes
      • 上士 — 10 minutes
  • 火焰炮
    • 普通伤害 decreased from 500-1300 to 450-1200 HP
  • 底盘
    • 升级 no longer affect 过速装置 charging over time. Now, the value of this parameter is always the same as the 最高 value of the parameter of each 底盘 before this update.
  • 无人机
    • 助推器
      • Additional 伤害道具启动加速度 increased from 10% - 20% to 10% - 25%
    • 守卫者
      • Additional 护甲道具启动加速度 increased from 10% - 80% to 10% - 90%
  • The 持续时间 of respawn 防护 decreased from 3 to 2 seconds
  • The 最低等级 to access 聊天 is decreased from 等级 3 (一等兵) to 等级 2 (二等兵)
  • Added an option to change your 昵称 for 免费 if you do it for the first time
  • Fixed the bugs with wrong 任务 progress on the 战斗 end screen


July 7th (Update 730)

  • Removed all modifications on 防护模块 but one
    • Their price is now 55 000 水晶
    • The total number of 水晶 you need to spend to 升级 1 模块 is 1 260 000 水晶
  • You can now see your 任务 progress in the 特殊 tab of the 战斗 end screen
    • You will only see a 任务 there if you contributed towards its progress in this 战斗
    • 每日 and 每周任务 are not yet supported
  • Improved the 公告 widget in the 大厅
  • Shortened 账号禁止原因 to meet the new requirements of 最高聊天 message length
  • Fixed the bug that let you leave a 战斗 while loading into it, making it impossible to search for a new 战斗


June 23rd (Update 728)

  • Added a system of hiding 任务 categories
    • You no longer see the Tutorial category after having completed all the 任务 in it
    • You will see the 活动 category during the whole 持续时间 of the 活动 (even after having completed all the 任务 in it)
    • You will always see 每日, 每周, 特殊, and Contract 任务 categories (even after having completed all the 任务 in them)
  • You now see the number of 任务 you haven’t completed yet for each 任务 category
  • HTML5 version got touch screen support and multiple changes to the UI for mobile devices
  • 火焰炮
    • 普通伤害 decreased from 140-350 to 125-325 HP/tick
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 140-400 to 150-375 HP/tick
    • 炮弹重装时间 increased from 2.0-1.0 to 2.0-1.5 sec
  • «脉冲星» 装备改造 no longer decrease the 暴击伤害几率 of any 炮塔
  • B0-NK 炮塔 now supports 维京’s 过速装置 effect
  • Added a warning screen informing about the need for a manual update of the desktop client for those who still use the older version of it, which does not support automatic updates.
  • Added a 特殊 version of the 每日坦克币通行证 offer with a 90% discount
    • Note: This 特殊 offer is only available for new 账号, registered after 23.06.2023. It can only be purchased once.

June 2nd (Update 726)

  • New XT 皮肤 for 维京 added to 超级礼盒
    • (Note) This is a new HD version of the 维京 XT 皮肤. The previous version will stay in the 车库 of its owners and will not be removed. We do see your requests about replacing the old XT 皮肤 with the new XT HD 皮肤. Though we understand your emotions, we cannot do it due to the huge difference in the costs of production between old and new 皮肤. Besides that, you often ask us to keep the old versions of 皮肤 instead of replacing them. Therefore, launching a new XT HD lineup of 皮肤 will be beneficial for everyone.
  • «精英通行证» added to the game as a temporary 活动. You will be able to obtain the new XT HD 皮肤 for 冰风暴. «精英通行证» has its own price and does not unlock the prizes in the usual 星级挑战.
    • (Note) This additional “星级挑战” is completed by earning or buying the same stars, and according to the same rules as the usual 星级挑战.
  • 滑膛炮
    • «脉冲星» 装备改造
      • Fixed the coefficient of decreasing shot reload 持续时间 when 维京’s 过速装置 is activated
  • 火箭炮
    • 暴击伤害几率 reduced from 26% to 20%
  • 模块
    • The 等级 at which 模块 become available increased from 中将 (25) to 上将 (26)
  • Updated the interface of the 星级挑战 screen
  • Updated the 3D model of the 球 in 橄榄球模式
  • «套件» section removed from the 商店 along with all the 套件
  • New «Early Access» section is added to the 商店, in which separate 炮塔 and 底盘 will be sold.
    • (Note) Availability of 炮塔 and 底盘 in this section 关注 the same rule as it did in 套件 — 7 等级 earlier than they become available in the 车库.
  • Added additional 礼包选项 for stars in the 商店

April 28th (Update 722)

      • Added a decrease of 暴击伤害几率 by -40%

      • The increase of 炮弹重装时间 changed from +10% to +50%

      • The decrease of barrel startup and slowdown time changed from -80% to -90%
  • 无人机
    • 等级 from which 无人机 become available changed from 军士长 (10) to 五级准尉 (11)
    • Mechanic — usage of additional 维修工具 reduced from 4 to 2
      • 半径 of effect increased from 20-25 to 20-30 meters; additional health points restored increased from 500-2000 to 1000-3000
  • 装备改造
    • 等级 from which 装备改造 become available changed from 五级准尉 (11) to 二级军士长 (8)
  • 防护模块
    • 等级 from which 模块 become available changed from 一级军士长 (9) to 三级准尉 (13)
  • Fixed a bug in 运动会模式专家战场, which was leading to increased 伤害 parameters when equipping certain 装备改造
  • Fixed the bug with the notification indicator dot in 任务 Categories.
  • Fixed the problem with images of 任务 Categories when the page is scaled down in the browser.
  • Fixed the issue with linebreak for titles of 任务 Categories.
  • Fixed the 过速装置 icons for 底盘 used in 特殊活动.


April 14th (Update 721)

  • A new 装备改造 for 镭射炮 has been added to 超级礼盒 — «燃烧瞄准镜».
    • (Note) This 装备改造 ignites the target on 暴击 arcade shots and on any sniper 模式 shots.
  • 活动任务 now disappear right when an 活动 ends.
    • (Note) It means you should claim 奖励 for 活动任务 before Monday morning (before the end date of the 活动), or they will disappear.
  • Updated the design of the 战斗 results screen
    • Instead of text buttons, we added buttons with icons to make it easier to understand which button will open the 车库 and which one will move you to the next 战斗.
    • Added a button to purchase «VIP 通行证»
  • Added 任务 categories system
    • When you open the «任务» screen, you will be shown the categories of 任务
    • There is a separate category for 任务 of each 活动 with a timer showing how much time there is left to complete them.
    • 星级挑战 are removed from this screen. To access them, you need to click on the 特殊 widget in the 大厅.
    • (Note) You will see some new categories of 任务, which have never been in the game before. We won’t tell you what these 任务 are and when new ones will be added. Keep an eye on our website and social media to be the first to find out.
  • 无人机 rebalance
    • The following 无人机 are removed from the game: 驱动器, 骑兵, 工程师, 奔跑者, 工兵, 供应, 突袭, 救生员, 爆破手, and 露营者.
    • 玩家 will get a compensation of 60% of the 水晶 they spent on upgrading the removed 无人机.
    • 电池 are removed from the game.
    • You will get compensation for all 电池 you had. For every 电池, you get 1 unit of each of the following 道具: 维修工具, 护甲提升, 伤害提升, and 速度提升.
    • (Note) Do not forget to check if you have a 无人机装备 before entering a 战斗 otherwise you will not have access to 道具!
  • Changes in the 升级 system
    • 升级 happen instantly now, no more need to wait or 速度 them up.
    • The 100% discount on the next modification of 装备 if the previous modification is fully upgraded, has been removed.
    • Added an option to use 坦克币 to 升级 when a 玩家 does not have enough 水晶.
    • Added a pop-up window to confirm before 升级.
    • The prices of upgrading Mk1-Mk6 modifications are the same for all 炮塔 and 底盘 now.
    • (Note) We have not changed the prices of 升级.
  • 火焰炮
    • 着火持续时间 changed from 1-10 to 1.5-5 seconds
    • Heating rate decreased from 0.2-0.4 to 0.15-0.3 temp/sec
  • 滑膛炮
    • 暴击伤害几率 increased from 10% to 13%
    • «突击弹药库» 装备改造
      • Shot reload 持续时间 decrease changed from -85% to -80%
      • Clip reload 持续时间 decrease changed from -50% to -40%
      • Added a decrease of 暴击伤害几率: -50%
  • 离子炮

  • 火龙珠

      • No longer decreases the 几率 of 暴击伤害
  • 极速炮

    • Barrel startup decreased from 1 to 0.75 sec
    • Barrel slowdown decreased from 1 to 0.75 sec

    • 暴击伤害几率 decreased from 4% to 2%

    • Coefficient of decreasing shot reload 持续时间 when 维京’s 过速装置 is activated changed from 0.4 to 0.3

    • No longer uses 电池
  • 双重身份验证 now works not for the 账号 of the 玩家, but for their device.

December 16th (Update #710)

  • A new 装备改造 for 蝎子 has been added to 超级礼盒 — «Armour-piercing shells»
    • (Note) This 装备改造 applies the «Armour-piercing» on 暴击 arcade shots and with each rocket.
  • 轰天炮
    • Fixed the bug when the «突击弹药» 装备改造 was dealing 暴击伤害, when it shouldn’t
    • «燃烧弹» 装备改造
      • 传奇装备改造 now, no longer available for 水晶 and is added to the «传奇» category of 幸运礼盒
  • 激光炮
    • 普通伤害 increased from 625-1250 to 670-1340 HP
    • Crticial 伤害 increased from 755-1510 to 935-1870 HP
    • 炮塔’s 伤害 now depends on the distance between you and a target.
      • 100% of 伤害 is dealt if the distance is less or equal to 80-100 m.
      • If the distance is between 80-100 m. and 120-150 m., the 伤害 is decreasing respectively.
      • If the distance is more than 120-150 m., 50% of the 最高伤害 is dealt.
      • (Note) We have argued for a long time about whether to introduce distance-based 伤害 reduction for the classic version of 激光炮. Our final decision is that without this feature, the 炮塔 turns out to be either extremely powerful at all distances or completely irrelevant at any distance, except for the large ones. This dependence of 伤害 on the distance to a target makes the 炮塔 be much more flexible in balancing. In the «运动会» 格式, the old version of this 炮塔 remains.
    • Changed the coefficient of the decrease of the 激光炮’s shot 炮弹重装时间 when 维京’s 过速装置 is activated from 0.25 to 0.3
      • (Note) This reduces the rate of fire increase
    • «稳定轮环» 装备改造
      • Removed the 普通伤害 increase
      • Added a 普通伤害 decrease of -5%
      • The 暴击伤害 decrease is changed from -9% to -32%
      • 伤害 is not distance-dependent
    • «Electromagnetic accelerator «侦察机» 装备改造
      • The 普通伤害 decrease is changed from -28% to -7%
      • The 暴击伤害 decrease is changed from -20% to -19%
      • The Shot warmup time decrease is changed from -25% to -30%
    • «不稳定轮环» 装备改造
      • The 暴击伤害 increase is changed from +100% to +80%
    • «大口径弹药» 装备改造
      • The 普通伤害 increase is changed from +20% to +12%
      • Added a 暴击伤害 increase of +7%
      • The 炮弹重装时间 increase changed from +50% to +15%
    • «Death Herald» compulsator» 装备改造
      • 传奇装备改造 now, no longer available for 水晶 and is added to the «传奇» category of 幸运礼盒
    • «超空间炮弹» 装备改造
      • 伤害 is not distance-dependent
  • 马格南
    • Changed the coefficient of the decrease of the 马格南’s shot 炮弹重装时间 when 维京’s 过速装置 is activated from 0.25 to 0.4
  • 战斗 interface is updated
    • The first one is where you have the main elements of the HUD at the corners of the screen. Health and reload bars are beneath your 坦克, and above them, we left a place for 道具 and 状态效果. This version is used for modern shooter games.
    • The second variant is where you have the main elements packed in the center of the screen and is more similar to the old one. The bars are located on the 坦克 and adapt to the game window’s width. Right below them, are the 道具 and 状态效果.
    • You can choose the best one in 设置.
    • (Note) The new TAB scoreboard is still in development.
  • Added an option for 道具 auto-activation. You can choose which 道具 to activate next, just press the button, and it will be activated for you automatically as soon as the 冷却 is over.
    • (Note) The main difference between Android and HTML versions of this feature is that we won’t activate your 道具 without your request, and they will only be consumed when needed.
  • Removed some in-战斗 notifications, so they do not overlap important elements of the interface and 其他坦克
  • Fixed the bug with the 大小 of a destroyed 坦克
    • (Note) Now it is not that small.

    • Projectile 速度 decreased from 350-350 to 300-350 m/sec.
    • (Note) Previously all modifications had the same value — 350. Now Mk1 has 300 and MkMAX has 350. 玩家 quite often confuse this writing of parameters with a spread of possible values, as if it would be a random value from this 射程. We no longer use random values from 射程, now this writing always means that the first number is a value for Mk1 and the second value is a value for MkMAX

    • «穿甲导弹» 装备改造
      • 持续时间 of the «护甲-Piercing» 状态效果 applied by a 暴击 hit is increased from 5 to 9 s.

September 23rd (Update #701)

    • (Note) This is an altered version of 火龙珠’s «爆破手» 射击效果 but with the color changed to match 离子炮’ traditional 射击效果. We recommend using it with the «等离子体涡轮加速器» 装备改造.
  • 轰天炮, 极速炮 and 雷暴炮
    • 射程 of 最低伤害 changed from 80-120 to 100-120 m.
    • (Note) This update mainly affects the Mk1 modifications of these 炮塔 and has no effect on the MAX modifications.
  • 镭射炮
    • «快速射击模式» 装备改造
      • No longer affects 射程 of 最低 and 最高伤害 in arcade 模式
      • (Note) There may be more changes to the parameters of this 装备改造 later. That's just how much it changes the 炮塔's gameplay.
  • Updated prices in the 商店 for some regions.


September 2nd (Update #699)

  • «蒸汽朋克» set of 皮肤 for 离子炮 and 猛犸象 added to the 超级礼盒
  • A 玩家 stops getting 经验值 once they 等级 up and until they leave the 战斗
    • (Note) This feature works only for the 匹配战斗. It is required to simplify the process of adding the contextual tutorial. It should prevent newcomers from getting new 等级 multiple times in the same 战斗.
  • 黑色森林匹配地图 is replaced with the updated 黑色森林匹配 Remastered version
  • The contextual tutorial is added to the game
    • (Note) To collect your feedback and to release the tutorial as soon as possible, we haven’t added the option to skip tutorial steps yet
  • 特殊 tutorial 任务 added to the game
    • For completing each of them, you get 1 普通幸运礼盒
    • For completing all of them, you get 100 坦克币
    • (Note) All 玩家 can obtain 奖励 for these 任务, not just the newcomers
  • First modifications of all 炮塔 and 底盘 can no longer be purchased in the 车库 for 水晶, except for the following 炮塔: 轰天炮, 离子炮 and 火焰炮, and for the following 底盘: 维京, 十字军 and 猎人中甲.
  • 火龙珠’s «赫利俄斯» 装备改造
    • Energy consumed per shot decrease changed from -10% to -15%
    • Energy recharge 速度 decreased by 27%
  • 火箭炮
    • «Missile launcher «猎人中甲» 装备改造
      • 瞄准 time decrease changed from -60% to -75%
      • 瞄准 recovery time decreased by 50%
    • «眩晕导弹» 装备改造
      • This 装备改造’s 设置 repeat 设置 of the «Missile launcher «猎人中甲» 装备改造
      • 暴击 hits can apply the «眩晕» 状态效果
      • 状态效果持续时间 increased from 0.4 s. to 1 s.
    • «穿甲导弹» 装备改造
      • This 装备改造’s 设置 repeat 设置 of the «Missile launcher «猎人中甲» 装备改造
      • 暴击 hits can apply the «护甲-Piercing» 状态效果
      • 状态效果持续时间 increased from 2 s. to 5 s.
  • 雷暴炮
    • «Hyperspeed» shells» 装备改造
      • Removed the -25% decrease of the 射程 of 最低伤害
  • 镭射炮
    • «快速射击模式» 装备改造
      • Energy recovery rate increase changed from +167% to +66%
      • Energy consumed per arcade shot decreased from 384 to 370.
      • 最高 sniping 伤害 decrease changed from -66% to -40%
  • The initial amount of 水晶 in a new 账号 changed from 1000 to 0 水晶
  • All default 防护模块 Mk1 and Mk2 are now available for the «一级军士长» 等级
  • «互夺军旗» and «Capture Points»  are now available for newcomers earlier than the «团队对战» 模式
  • The 每周 «Get into the TOP-3» 任务 is removed. You can no longer get it.
  • Fixed the bug with Chaos 伤害 being counted as 暴击伤害 in 任务
  • Now inactive 账号 need to play 3 战斗 in order to get access, not only to the 大厅聊天 but to the 战斗聊天 too.


August 26th (Update #698)

  • New 皮肤 added to the updated 超级礼盒 — 蝎子 XT
  • The «蝎子» 炮塔 added to the 普通幸运礼盒 in «史诗» category. With this update, your current and 普通幸运礼盒 will become old 普通幸运礼盒. You can only get 蝎子 from 幸运礼盒 you obtain after the release.
  • 特斯拉
    • 暴击伤害几率 increased from 12% to 16%
  • 电磁炮
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 665-1330 to 580-1160 HP
    • 暴击伤害几率 increased from 12% to 16%
    • 伤害狙击模式 decreased from 900-1800 to 850-1700
    • 炮弹重装时间狙击模式 increased from 4.2-2.8 to 6.6-4.8 s.
    • 瞄准 time decreased from 3-2 to 1.5-0.6 s.
    • 瞄准 recovery time decreased from 0.7 to 0.6 s.
    • 射程 of max 伤害 increased from 60-80 to 80-100 m.
    • 射程 of min 伤害 increased from 80-120 to 120-150 m.
    • Weak 伤害 percentage increased from 25% to 50%
    • «电磁齐射» and «穿甲齐射» 装备改造 can now apply 状态效果 not only with 齐射 shots but with 暴击伤害 too
    • (Note) 电磁炮 will significantly change after this update, and here is why. 电磁炮 was supposed to be a mobile sniper. Instead, we got a version that needs to stop and stand in a place for a long time to aim. 瞄准 in 移动 takes time, and the target hold time is too short. We got this version after a batch of changes that were needed to fix 其他 problems. For example, when we added 装备改造 for this 炮塔, we wanted 玩家 to use the 炮塔 this way: you deal most of the 伤害 with a 齐射 shot and finish them with an arcade shot. Therefore, a variant with a long reload after a 齐射 was not used, because then the 状态效果 would definitely finish before the 炮塔 reload. Now for all status-related 装备改造, we add an option to apply 状态效果 with 暴击 shots, randomly, and you can still apply it guaranteed (for example, with a 颗粒 from the last shot of 滑膛炮 or with a 齐射 of 电磁炮). Thus, it became possible to implement the combination with finishing opponents in the reverse order. First, the enemy receives 暴击伤害 with a 状态效果 applied, and then you finish them with a 齐射. Thanks to this model, now the 电磁炮炮塔 can be returned to the original idea of being a mobile sniper. It will not take much time to aim and 射击 a 齐射, but the 炮弹重装时间 got increased. If earlier 电磁炮 was similar in gameplay to 镭射炮, now it will be more like 激光炮. With an interesting addition. If a 玩家 carefully monitors the amount of 伤害 dealt to a target and the use of the «维修工具» 道具, then the 玩家 will always be able to make the right decision when to finish the target with a 齐射 and safely retire for a long 冷却.
  • 镭射炮
    • 射程 of max 伤害 increased from 60-80 to 80-100 m.
    • 射程 of min 伤害 increased from 80-120 to 120-150 m.
    • Weak 伤害 percentage increased from 25% to 50%
  • Game 模式
    • The number of points your 团队 gets for capturing a 旗子 in the 突袭 (突袭) 模式 increased from 6 to 10
    • (Note) After adding a huge delay before removing a destroyed 坦克 from a 地图, it became easier to defend your base in this 模式. Increasing the number of points for an attacking 团队 should compensate for this.
  • 专家战场聊天 improvements
    • Removed the following 聊天 channels for the 专家战场格式:
      • Classic
      • 激光炮
      • 运动会
      • 跑酷
    • When you enter the game, the «上将» 聊天 channel is opened by default
    • When you leave a 专家战场, the «上将» 聊天 channel is opened by default
  • 猛犸象’s 过速装置 can now move destroyed 坦克
    • (Note) To make this 过速装置 work as it is designed to work, we decided to add a feature of throwing away destroyed 坦克 when in contact with them. This looks so 史诗, you can now juggle with enemy 坦克.
  • The «Jack-in-the-箱子» effect now also appears when finishing an opponent with Chaos 伤害
    • (Note) Did you think that we added Chaos 伤害 to add 防护 from 过速装置 later? Huh! We just enjoy how cool it looks when 炮塔 fly.

August 5th (Update #695)

  • New 装备改造 for 雷暴炮 added to the updated 超级礼盒 — «山顶城堡» shells
    • (Note) With each shot, this 装备改造 applies the «干扰器» 状态效果 to all the affected targets for 3 seconds. Only direct shots apply the 状态效果
  • New 装备改造 for 火焰炮 added to the 传奇 category of the updated 普通幸运礼盒: 磁性混合物, 麻痹混合物, 有毒混合物, and 干扰混合物
  • Added «Megagold» — a 珍奇金箱子 that gives you 10 000 水晶
    • (Note) This type of 金箱子 is available in all 匹配战斗, not only in just 活动模式. However, it appears only during some 特殊活动 like Discount Weekend
  • Added the «Jack-in-the-箱子» effect
  • Changed color indication of 伤害 types. Now, Orange color means 暴击伤害 and Red implies that a target is destroyed. You can observe that a target is destroyed with the 暴击伤害 by seeing the «Jack-in-the-箱子» effect in action
  • 高原地图 got the day 主题 back
    • (Note) 傍晚 version will be added as a separate 主题 in one of the upcoming updates
  • Added 夜晚主题 for all 匹配地图
    • (Note) Except 圣地之战. Instead of a 夜晚主题, there will be an 傍晚 one
  • Reduced the contrast between dark and light areas on the 夜晚主题地图
    • (Note) 夜晚 is more like 傍晚 now! We hope that it be will much more comfortable to play on 夜晚地图 now
  • Increased the delay before removing a 底盘 after the 坦克 is destroyed
    • (Note) Once upon a time, 坦克 did not disappear immediately after being destroyed, and the tactic of blocking opponents with a destroyed 底盘 was a good one. With the introduction of the «Jack-in-the-箱子» effect, we had to increase the delay so that the detached 炮塔 has time to return from the flight and hit the ground. We decided to increase the 持续时间 when a destroyed 坦克 remains on the ground to the 最高 possible (until a new 坦克 appears) to explore all the gameplay possibilities of this mechanic.
    • It will be unusual to play this version of the game, but we ask you to take the change as seriously as possible. Evaluate both pros and cons of such 设置. We will be reading your feedback closely.
  • 滑膛炮
    • 暴击 hit 几率 decreased from 12% to 10%
    • «Dragon Breath» 装备改造
      • The 启动加速度 of setting fire to an opponent on 暴击 hits decreased from 100% to 40%.
      • No longer decreases 暴击伤害
    • «飞龙’s Breath» 装备改造
      • Applies the «冷冻» 状态效果: both on 暴击 hit and by a 颗粒 from the last shot in the clip
      • No longer decreases clip reload 持续时间
    • «磁性颗粒» 装备改造
      • Applies the «电磁脉冲» 状态效果: both on 暴击 hit and by a 颗粒 from the last shot in the clip
      • No longer decreases clip reload 持续时间
    • «眩晕颗粒» 装备改造
      • Applies the «眩晕» 状态效果: both on 暴击 hit and by a 颗粒 from the last shot in the clip
      • No longer decreases clip reload 持续时间
      • 持续时间 of the «眩晕» 状态效果 is decreased from 2 seconds to 1 second
    • «穿甲射击» 装备改造
      • Applies the «护甲-Piercing» 状态效果: both on 暴击 hit and by a 颗粒 from the last shot in the clip
      • No longer decreases clip reload 持续时间
    • «干扰射击» 装备改造
      • Applies the «干扰器» 状态效果: both on 暴击 hit and by a 颗粒 from the last shot in the clip
      • 持续时间 of the «干扰器» 状态效果 is decreased from 5 seconds to 3 seconds
      • No longer decreases clip reload 持续时间
  • 雷暴炮
    • «Hyperspeed» shells» 装备改造
      • The decrease in tange of 最低伤害 changed from -50% to -25%
      • Projectile 速度 increased from +100% to +200%
  • 电磁炮
    • Projectile 速度 increased from 200 m/s to 300 m/s
    • 后坐力 in arcade 模式 decreased from 1,1-2,2 to 1,0-2,0
    • Enabled 聊天 between 团队. Use the «TAB» key to switch between 聊天模式
  • Added a new type of 伤害 — «Chaos» 伤害
    • This type of 伤害 can neither be increased by 助推器 nor can be decreased by 防护
    • The following entities inflict the «Chaos» 伤害:
      • 黄蜂轻甲’s 过速装置
      • 霍珀’s 过速装置
      • 十字军’s 过速装置
      • 猎人中甲’s 过速装置
      • 阿瑞斯’ 过速装置
      • 猛犸象’s 过速装置
      • Exploding a 坦克 with the «爆破手» 无人机
      • 金箱子 meteorite
    • Added a 特殊 icon for «Chaos» 伤害»
    • (Note) 霍珀’s, 猎人中甲’s and 十字军’s 过速装置 already had the same rules as «Chaos» 伤害. The introduction of «Chaos» 伤害 won’t affect them in any way, but now they work the same way as 其他过速装置.
  • Fixed the bug that was making it impossible to create an 匹配小组 for 玩家 who play the game on partner websites
  • You can now choose which 模式 to play right after you click on the «Play» button
  • Added an auto scroll for list of 战斗 and list of 地图主题 in 专家战场
  • Changed the design of additional 设置 screen in 专家战场
  • The step of calculating the angle of automatic horizontal aim for mobile 玩家 has been reduced from 1 to 0.5 degrees
    • (Note) It means that 最高 horizontal aim angle is decreased by two: from 4 to 2 degrees
  • Updated the 旗子, now with the new 3D坦克 logo

April 22nd (Update #684)

  • A new 装备改造 for 火龙珠 has been added to 超级礼盒 — «低温领域».
    • (Note) Just like 喷雾器 ignites a target, this new 装备改造冰风暴 it. We have seen your comments that these 装备改造 should also have an explosion or 火龙珠. We might add such features in the 未来世界.
  • The 最高 number of 玩家 per 小组 has been decreased from 4 to 3.
    • (Note) We have conducted a study to find out how often 坦克手 play in 小组 of 4 and asked their opinion about such 小组 in 匹配. After analyzing the results and taking into 账号 that the 匹配 system works better when the 最高小组大小 is lower, we have decided to reduce the 最高 number of 玩家 in a 小组 from 4 to 3.
  • 持续时间 of 维修工具’s 防护 from 状态效果 decreased from 1 to 0.9 s.
    • (Note) Longer 防护 from 状态效果 duplicates the functions of 底盘 immunity 装备改造. Thus we do not see any 原因 to increase the 持续时间. Instead, we are decrease the 持续时间 to emphasize not only a new feature of the 维修工具 but also to make its use more 能力-dependent.
  • Added lighting for headlights and lamps on 炮塔 and 底盘
  • 磁力炮
    • 暴击伤害 (not 治疗) 几率 decreased from 12% to 7%.
  • 轰天炮
    • «精确弹药装载» 装备改造
    • The first shot after respawn is 暴击;
    • Fixed the bug when you 射击 to the sky and it doesn’t update 暴击几率 counter. It caused the «精确弹药装载» 装备改造 to function incorrectly.
  • 雷暴炮

But 溅射伤害 is no longer dependent on distance, and you always deal 60% of 伤害 if your 溅射伤害 reached the opponent. We hope that it will make shooting at the ground and obstacles a more viable tactic.

April 8th (Update 683)

  • A new 装备改造 for 火龙珠 has been added to 超级礼盒 — «赫利俄斯».
    • (Note) This 装备改造 doesn’t apply any 状态效果 and doesn’t increase 暴击伤害几率. With this 装备改造, this is no longer 火龙珠.

This is a new sniper plasma-gun. It significantly increases both 射程 and rate of fire. You only have enough energy for 7 shots which are launched as a continuous burst at the target. You need to play this new 火龙珠 in a completely different way.

  • 维修工具 now can remove all applied 状态效果 and protect from 状态效果 for 1 second
    • (Note) It may seem that one second is not enough. Maybe. But even one second may be enough to make some 过速装置 completely useless against you. We will keep an eye on how you use this new feature.
  • 火龙珠

April 1st (Update 682)

  • A new 装备改造 for 离子炮 added to the 超级礼盒 — «等离子体干扰器».
    • [Note] This 装备改造 slightly increases the 射程 of fire and applies the 干扰器状态效果 for 1 second on each hit.
  • 战斗团队聊天 are enabled. You still cannot 聊天 with opponents.
    • [Note] We realize that communication is important for you. We return the 战斗聊天, but for now in a limited form. If we notice an increase in the number of violations of the rules, we will be forced to disable 聊天 again.
  • Bonus 箱子 parachutes are replaced with cargo 无人机.
    • [Note] As yet we have not provided for the possibility of standing on 无人机 ;).

      • Shot reload increase is now 10% instead of 15%;
    • «等离子焰炬» 装备改造
      • Projectile 速度 decrease is now 40% instead of 35%;
    • «狂暴» 装备改造
      • Instead of +20% increase of energy used per shot, shot reload 持续时间 decreased by 25%.
        • [Note] Previously, this 装备改造 only gave you an opportunity to 射击 without reloading. Now it's both: no recharge and increased rate of fire! This change should make 狂暴's performance be the same as for 其他装备改造.
  • 火箭炮:
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 900-1800 to 850-1700 HP.
  • 雷暴炮:
    • 暴击伤害 increased from 405-810 to 450-900 HP.
    • 冲击力 increased from 2-5 to 2-6 units.
  • 终结者:
    • 激光炮炮塔炮弹重装时间 increased from 1.4-1.2 to 1.8-1.5 sec.;
    • Time to reach max rocket 速度 decreased from 2 to 1.5 sec.;
    • [Note] Seeing the results of the latest changes, we came to the conclusion that it is worth making 剑圣's fire 模式 have even more different roles. 激光炮 barrels are now designed to fire at long 射程 and take more time to reload. And 火箭炮 missiles should slow down even faster to remain as useful as possible only in close combat.

March 18th (Update 681)

  • A new 装备改造 for 火焰炮 added to the 超级礼盒 — «磁性混合物».
    • [Note] 设置 are pretty similar to 麻痹混合物装备改造. The 持续时间 of the «电磁脉冲» 状态效果 applied on 暴击 shots is 2 seconds.
  • 战斗聊天 are disabled.
    • [Note] We temporarily disable 聊天 in 战斗 as it became harder to moderate them in time in the current climate. 大厅聊天 are still available.
  • 火龙珠:
    • 暴击伤害 increased from 170-340 to 270-540 HP
    • 每次射击能量 increased from 69-60 to 220-180 eng/shot
    • Recharge 速度 increased from 50 to 230 eng/sec
    • The number of shots until being out of energy decreased from 29-30 to 14-15
    • [Note] The previous changes in the 火龙珠 parameters solved the efficiency problems but made the 炮塔 be too similar to 离子炮. Your energy was almost unlimited. New 设置 should still keep the 炮塔 efficient while there is energy and should bring it back to work much faster after running out of energy. We hope that this update will make 离子炮 be the 炮塔 responsible for “spamming” opponents with shots and 火龙珠 to be the 炮塔 for precise shots to a single opponent at the same distance.
  • 火龙珠’s «不稳定等离子体» 装备改造
    • Projectile 速度 increased by 20%
    • The 装备改造’s price increased from 149 000 to 245 000 水晶
  • 火龙珠’s «等离子焰炬» 装备改造
    • 每次射击能量 decreased by 30%
  • 装备 change 冷却 increased from 11 to 12 minutes.
  • 装备 change 冷却 decreased from 11 to 10 minutes in 专家战场.
  • 装备 change 冷却 is removed for 跑酷模式战斗.
  • Added the 昵称 change form for inactive 账号.

  • A new 装备改造 for 冰风暴 added to the 超级礼盒 — «麻痹混合物».
    • [Note] Adds a paralyzing mixture into the cooling agent. A 暴击 concentration of the mixture may cause all the target's systems to be paralyzed. 冷冻启动加速度 and 暴击伤害 reduced.

    • 团队剑圣 — 30 seconds;
    • JGR — no delay.

    • [Note] It is now more efficient to play with 滑膛炮 without being close to an opponent. When you 射击 at the *最高 distance, 伤害 will be the same as if you 射击 at close 射程.
  • 装备 change 冷却 increased from 10 to 11 minutes.

    • [Note] No changes to the «Take one of the top three places in the winner's 团队 in 1 战斗» 任务.
  • Fixed the bug with 剑圣 getting self-destroyed after becoming a 剑圣 when you are in the 车库.
    • [Note] A 玩家 can no longer become a 剑圣 while being in the 车库.

  • The feature to get bonuses for watching ads in the mobile version of the game is disabled due to the lack of opportunity to ensure the stability of its operation for all users.

    • Red outline — the target is at 最高伤害射程;
    • Orange outline — the target is at a distance where your 伤害 decreases when distance increase;
    • Yellow outline — the target is further from the optimal distance and will only get minimal 伤害;
    • Gray outline — the target is protected during respawn and won’t get 伤害;
    • Bold outline — the 炮塔 is reloaded and ready to 射击;
    • Thin outline — the 炮塔 is reloading.
    • [Note] We've analyzed your feedback from the last update where we changed the target highlighting and agree that **the colour of the outline should show how far the target is and how much of the 伤害 it will get. January 28th (Update 677)

  • Added a new 装备改造 into 超级礼盒: 离子炮’ «等离子体涡轮加速器» 装备改造
    • Note: This 装备改造 significantly increases both rate and 射程 of fire. Main 伤害 will be being dealt with 暴击 hits.
  • Added new 特价优惠 to the 商店’s 展示:
    • 幸运礼盒 ×1 – 1230 水晶;
    • 维修工具 ×30 – 225 水晶;
    • 护甲提升 ×30 – 75 水晶;
    • 伤害提升 ×30 – 75 水晶;
    • 速度提升 ×30 – 75 水晶;
    • 地雷 ×30 – 75 水晶.
  • Paid 展示刷新 is no longer available. The 展示 is refreshed automatically every day.
  • All the old 特价优惠 are removed from the 商店’s 展示.
    • Note: You also no longer can get 装备套件 from the 商店’s 展示. However, the 套件 will be returned later with the «Contracts» system that will be added to the 商店 in the new interface. Stay tuned!
  • Added a 1.1s delay before shooting for all 过速装置 except 黄蜂轻甲’s one.
    • Note: Now 玩家 will need to plan their actions in advance before using an 过速装置. This way 玩家 can show their 能力 of using 过速装置. Perhaps some 过速装置 may become weaker. We will watch how 坦克手 adapt to the changes and make adjustments if needed.
  • All the 底盘 except 黄蜂轻甲 lose 50% of the 过速装置 charge in case its launch was interrupted.
  • The «电磁脉冲» 状态效果 now only forces «维修工具» and «地雷» 道具 to reload when their remaining 冷却 time is less than the 持续时间 of the applied effect.
    • Note: In 其他 words, applying the «电磁脉冲» 状态效果 will not 速度 up 红队’ reload of «维修工具» and «地雷» 道具.
  • 火箭炮’s «眩晕导弹» 装备改造:
    • Only one opponent is stunned, the one that was hit by the rocket.
  • 霍珀:
    • Jump 启动加速度 increased by 10%;
    • 最高 height of jumps increased by 30-40%;
    • Slightly increased vertical stabilization 启动加速度;
      • Note: The change doesn’t affect flight stabilization but improves stabilization when moving over uneven ground.
    • Distance between the 底盘 and ground decreased from 0.8 to 0.3m.
  • 圣骑士:
    • The 坦克 can now flip over when falling off a cliff;
    • Distance between the 底盘 and ground decreased from 0.75 to 0.3m.
  • 十字军:
    • The 坦克 can now flip over when falling off a cliff;
    • Distance between the 底盘 and ground decreased from 0.75 to 0.3m.
  • 阿瑞斯:
    • The 坦克 can now flip over when falling off a cliff;
    • Distance between the 底盘 and ground decreased from 0.75 to 0.3m;
    • 过速装置伤害/治疗半径 increased to 10m;
    • The 射程 of mutual detonation of 球 of different 团队 is 5m.;
  • Item availability per 等级 changes:
    • «驱动器», «骑兵», and «工程师» 无人机 — available starting from the «军士长» 等级;
    • «奔跑者», «工兵», and «供应» 无人机 — available starting from the «二级准尉» 等级;
    • «突袭», «救生员», and «Mechanic» 无人机 — available starting from the «中尉» 等级;
    • «爆破手», «破坏者», and «露营者» 无人机 — available starting from the «上校» 等级;
    • «助推器», «守卫者», and «魔术师» 无人机 — available starting from the «上将» 等级;
    • «亥伯龙神» 无人机 — available starting from the «大元帅» 等级;
    • «地雷» 道具 — available starting from the «一等兵» 等级;
    • «速度提升» 道具 — available starting from the «下士» 等级;
    • «护甲提升» 道具 — available starting from the «中士» 等级;
    • «伤害提升» 道具 — available starting from the «上士» 等级;
    • 水晶箱子 in 战斗 are replaced with 道具 starting from the «二级军士长» 等级;
    • «电池» 道具 — available starting from the «军士长» 等级;
    • 装备改造 are available in the 车库 and 幸运礼盒 starting from the «五级准尉» 等级.
  • In the «军团» section, searching for 玩家 through a 特殊 menu can now be used by pressing the «Enter» 键盘 button.
  • Fixed the bug in the mobile version with 坦克 physics where two 球 lightnings would self-destruct on the 地图.
  • Changed the way the anti-cheat system reacts to 移动, jumps, and flights in the «跑酷» 模式.


January 21st (Update 676)

January 14th (Update 675)

  • Added a new 装备改造 into 超级礼盒: 离子炮’ «构造等离子体» 装备改造
    • (Note) This 装备改造 applies a micro «眩晕» effect to an opponent with each 暴击 shot. The micro «眩晕» effect is less effective in stopping opponents than the normal one but can be used to disable some abilities that take time to be activated (some 过速装置 and 极速炮’s barrel startup)
  • When 瞄准 at an opponent, you will now see an indication of 炮塔 reloading. Red outlines indicate that your 炮塔 is ready to 射击, and orange outlines show that your 炮塔 is still reloading.
    • (Note) We are interested in your feedback about this feature. It might be useful against 特斯拉, 镭射炮, 电磁炮, 雷暴炮, etc.
  • 普通幸运礼盒 have been updated
    • Updated rarity 小组几率
      • The 几率 to get a 普通 item is 50%
      • The 几率 to get an 稀有 item is 34%
      • The 几率 to get a 珍奇 item is 10%
      • The 几率 to get an 史诗 item is 5%
      • The 几率 to get a 传奇 item is 1%
      • 异国情调 items are no longer found in 普通幸运礼盒
    • Updated the list of items available from 普通幸运礼盒
      • Removed 金箱子, VIP 通行证, 皮肤, and sets of 道具
      • Added 传奇装备改造 that were only available in 超级礼盒
      • Added 射击效果 and 迷彩 that were only available in 超级礼盒 or 星级挑战
      • Added base modifications of all 炮塔, 底盘, and 无人机 (except 布鲁特斯 and 危机)
    • Updated the different ways of getting 普通幸运礼盒
      • 特殊任务 to 等级 up now 奖励 you with 1 普通幸运礼盒
      • 特殊每日任务 for VIP 通行证 owners now 奖励 you with 1 普通幸运礼盒
      • 水晶 and 道具 have now been replaced with 1 普通幸运礼盒 in the 每日任务 prizes
    • (Note) It will now be much easier to get updated 普通幸运礼盒 after this update, and you will have access to new 炮塔装备改造 from 普通幸运礼盒.
  • Updated 超级礼盒
    • Updated rarity 小组几率
      • The 几率 to get a 普通 item is <1%
      • The 几率 to get an 稀有 item is 67%
      • The 几率 to get a 珍奇 item is 20%
      • The 几率 to get an 史诗 item is 10%
      • The 几率 to get a 传奇 item is 2%
      • The 几率 to get an 异国情调 item is <1%
    • (Note) Now, 几率 to get cool items from 超级礼盒 are twice as likely as getting them from 普通幸运礼盒. 异国情调 items will be items that are available for the 持续时间 of an ongoing 活动 (new 装备改造, 皮肤, 装备 that are released as a part of an 活动)
  • Passive income of 礼盒碎片 disabled
    • We have abandoned our plans on developing 礼盒碎片 in favor of giving more 幸运礼盒. The 幸运礼盒 you were getting from 礼盒碎片 every day can now be received for completing 每日任务.
  • 火焰炮:
    • Ordinary 伤害 increased from 240-740 to 380-1060;
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 500-1500 to 380-1060;
    • 射程 of max 伤害 decreased from 10-10 to 7-10 m.;
    • 暴击伤害几率 decreased from 20% to 12%;
    • Energy consumption increased from 200 to 333 (eng/sec);
    • Energy Recharge 持续时间 decreased from 6 to 1 sec;
    • 锥角 decreased from 30 to 20 (º);
    • 火焰炮’s «高压泵» 装备改造:
      • 射程 of max 伤害 increased by 50%;
      • 射程 of min 伤害 increased by 50%;
      • Price increased to 245 000 水晶;
    • 火焰炮’s «紧凑型坦克» 装备改造:
      • Heating rate is always 100%;
      • 温度极限 is always 100%;
      • 炮弹重装时间 doubled;
    • 火焰炮’s «燃烧混合物» 装备改造:
      • No longer affects energy consumption;
      • Ordinary 伤害 change increased by 20% instead of 50%;
      • 暴击伤害 change increased by 20% instead of 50%;
    • (Note) These changes are needed not only to buff 火焰炮 but also to make its gameplay different from that of 冰风暴. The faster energy reload is reminiscent of the old 火焰炮, where you needed to rely on the afterburn effect. This version of 火焰炮 will deplete its fuel faster, forcing you to make a decision on whether to attack the target again or to rely on the afterburn effect.
  • 冰风暴:
    • Ordinary 伤害 increased from 450-900 to 500-1000;
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 1800-3600 to 1500-3000;
    • 射程 of max 伤害 decreased from 10-10 to 7-10 m.;
    • Rate of 冷冻 (temp/sec) decreased from 0,6 to 0,2-0,5;
    • 锥角 decreased from 30 to 20 (º);
    • 冰风暴’s «震动冻结» 装备改造:
      • No longer affects energy consumption;
      • 冷冻 rate is always 100%;
      • No longer deal 暴击伤害;
    • (Note) We are slightly moving focus from 暴击 to ordinary 伤害. We are glad that you like the new 冰风暴, but we needed to moderately nerf it in order to keep balance.
  • 特斯拉:
    • Chain lightning reload increased from 0.9 to 1 (s);
    • 特斯拉’s «吸热闪电» 装备改造:
      • Lightning 球伤害 decrease changed from -50% to -75%;
      • Lightning 球 warmup time doubled;
    • 特斯拉’s «超导发射» 装备改造:
      • Lightning 球伤害 decrease changed from -50% to -75%;
      • Lightning 球 warmup time doubled;
    • 特斯拉’s «Armour-piercing discharge» 装备改造:
      • Lightning 球伤害 decrease changed from -50% to -75%;
      • Lightning 球 warmup time doubled;
    • 特斯拉’s «干扰发射» 装备改造:
      • Lightning 球伤害 decrease changed from -50% to -75%;
      • Lightning 球 warmup time doubled;
    • (Note) These 装备改造 apply 状态效果 and the idea behind them is to use them at long distances. However, 玩家 found it more useful to use these 装备改造 at melee 射程. Therefore, we had to nerf them as they were too effective in the melee 射程.
  • 火箭炮:
    • 火箭炮’s «眩晕导弹» 装备改造:
    • The «眩晕» effect 持续时间 decreased from 2 to 0.5 s.;
    • 瞄准 time reduction increased from 50% to 80%;
    • 齐射炮弹重装时间 increased by 40%;
    • (Note) The previous version of the stunning 火箭炮 could immobilize a target too easily. We have replaced the 眩晕状态效果 with the Micro-眩晕状态效果, similar to the one that the new 离子炮装备改造 gives.
  • 圣骑士:
    • 暴击伤害防护 during 过速装置 disabled.
    • (Note) The idea behind 圣骑士’s 过速装置 was that 十字军’s 过速装置 would be the main counter to it. Unfortunately, much fewer 玩家 use 十字军 than 圣骑士, so we have decided to let the 过速装置 of 蜂王 and 维京, the most popular 底盘 in the game, be effective against 圣骑士’s 过速装置.
  • 底盘装备改造:
    • Prices of «轻型结构» and «重型结构» 装备改造 are now at 245 000 水晶 instead of 4990 坦克币.
  • 装备 change time increased from 7 to 8 minutes;
  • 专家战场
    • 专家战场 are available starting from the 上士等级;
    • 运动会 and Classic 格式 are added to 专家战场, but you cannot earn 水晶 or 经验值 in them (like in the 跑酷模式);
    • Removed DR, 经验值, and BP 格式. The 经验值/BP 格式 is kept;
  • Updated 商店 prices for particular countries.

December 3rd (Update 671)

  • Updated the standard 皮肤 for 离子炮 to the HD version
  • Updated the shot 声音 effects of 离子炮
  • Added new 装备改造 for 离子炮 — «喷雾器», available in 超级礼盒
    • 暴击伤害 ignites a target with a limit of 50% of the 最高 temperature.
    • Projectile 速度 is reduced by 45%.
  • Updated the effects inflicted by «干扰器»
    • In addition to blocking 过速装置 activation, it now also disables 无人机 and, if applicable, their boosted effects for the entire 持续时间 of the 状态效果.
    • 无人机 «布鲁特斯» and «亥伯龙神» are immune to this effect.
    • With this change, 干扰器 becomes comparable in strength to 其他状态效果. «干扰器» is now an «antidote» to most 无人机. Popular 无人机 like 守卫者 and 助推器 are obviously weakened. 危机 loses its ability to enhance 道具 and will instead function like 布鲁特斯. And 无人机 such as «爆破手» and «救生员» will not be able to perform their functions if they are disabled by the 干扰器 effect.
  • Added «抗干扰器» 装备改造 to the 车库 for purchase.
  • Added «抗干扰器» 装备改造 to 幸运礼盒.
  • Updated the «冷冻» 状态效果
    • In addition to slowing down enemy 坦克, it now also disables 伤害提升 effects for the entire 持续时间 of the 状态效果.
    • This 状态效果 was the weakest one. Increasing the slowdown effect is not the solution to this problem. Instead, we strengthened this 状态效果 by adding a mechanism similar to the 护甲-Piercing 状态效果’s capabilities. Instead of disabling additional 护甲, it disables the effect of 伤害提升. This change will increase the role of both 冷冻装备改造 and the 冰风暴炮塔 itself, especially when used for defensive roles. Share your feedback about the new «冷冻» 状态效果!
    • When taking a bonus 箱子, a 无人机 will activate only if it depends on the 道具 offered by the bonus 箱子.
    • Activating a 无人机 this way is similar to activating a 无人机 by using 道具 from your 车库. For example, if you have the 守卫者无人机装备, and you take a 护甲提升 bonus 箱子, the 无人机 will be activated.
  • Updated the «露营者» 无人机
    • Now the 无人机 increases 伤害 by 60% and 护甲 by 90% when your 坦克 has full health.
    • Once you receive 伤害, the 无人机 starts reloading and will keep on reloading until your 坦克 has fully recharged its health points.
    • The 无人机 also reduces 维修工具冷却 when using 道具.
    • The old version of the 无人机 was not popular at all. Please note that the enhanced 护甲 only protects the 坦克 from the first oncoming 伤害 received when «露营者» is activated. This makes the 无人机 effective against 其他露营者, but almost useless against 炮塔 with rapid fire rates.
  • Updated the «工程师» 无人机
    • Now the 无人机 repairs all 坦克 in a small 半径 around itself if any of these 坦克 picks up a bonus 箱子.
    • The previous version of «工程师» on 高等级 could spoil teammates’ tactics for using their 无人机.
  • Updated the «供应» 无人机
    • Now the 无人机 does not extend the 持续时间 of its own 道具.
    • The 持续时间 of the 道具 shared with 蓝队 is reduced.
    • Shared 护甲提升 and 伤害提升 will activate the effects of allied 守卫者 and 助推器 respectively.
    • The previous version of the «供应» 无人机 had problems similar to that of the «工程师» 无人机.
  • Updated the «亥伯龙神» 无人机
    • Now the 无人机 accelerates 冷却 of 道具, including 维修工具 and 地雷.
  • Updated the «魔术师» 无人机
    • 底盘 acceleration is reduced from +30% to +10%.
    • Enhancement to 速度提升 remains unchanged.
  • Updated the «危机» 无人机
    • Now taking 奖励箱 does not change the 道具 boosted at the time.
    • 底盘 acceleration is reduced from +30% to +10%.
    • Enhancement to 速度提升 remains unchanged.
  • Updated the «火焰炮» 炮塔
    • 最高伤害射程 is increased from 7 meters to 10 meters.
  • Updated 特斯拉’s «干扰发射» 装备改造
    • The «干扰器» 状态效果持续时间 is reduced from 15 seconds to 7 seconds.
  • Updated 离子炮’s «Stable plasma» 装备改造
    • Projectile 速度 is increased by 20%.
    • 冲击力 is increased by 20%.
    • Price of 装备改造 is increased to 245,000 水晶.
  • Updated 火龙珠’s «等离子焰炬» 装备改造
    • 后坐力 is now reduced by 50% rather than 80%.
  • Updated the «火箭炮» 炮塔
    • Vertical aim-assist is increased from 9 degrees to 45 degrees.
    • This 允许 the 炮塔 to destroy flying targets.
  • Updated the «极速炮» 炮塔
    • Vertical aim-assist is increased from 9 degrees to 45 degrees.
    • 冲击力 is increased from 0.5-1 to 1-2.
    • This 允许 the 炮塔 to destroy flying targets.
  • Updated the «激光炮» 炮塔
    • Reloading time is increased from 3.3-2.6 seconds to 4.4-2.6 seconds;
  • Updated the «不稳定轮环» 装备改造
    • 暴击伤害 is increased by 26%.
    • Standard 伤害 is decreased by 50%.
    • 冲击力 is no longer increased.
    • The previous version of the 设置 dealt with the problem of the excessive efficiency of the 装备改造 but also raised many questions when used with the «增压» 状态效果. To avoid confusion, the 设置 were changed to a version with lower 伤害 spread.
  • Updated the «超空间炮弹» 装备改造
    • 普通伤害伤害 bonus is increased from +40% to +45%.
    • 冲击力 reduction is increased from -25% to -30%.
  • Updated the «黄蜂轻甲» 底盘
    • The 持续时间 of the «干扰器» 状态效果 applied by its 炸弹 is decreased from 30 seconds to 9 seconds.
    • This is due to the updated effect of 干扰器 on 无人机.
  • Updated the «霍珀» 底盘
    • 过速装置 charge 持续时间 is decreased from 180 seconds to 150 seconds.
    • 持续时间 of the «眩晕» 状态效果 is increased from 1 second to 3 seconds.
    • The 最高 angle at which the 底盘 remains controllable has been increased from 20 degrees to 180 degrees.
    • Force of stabilizers is reduced from 10 to 6.
    • 最高 angle of list is increased from 60 degrees to 360 degrees.
    • 霍珀's 底盘 is no longer able to effectively stabilize itself during flight. Any hit by an enemy shot, takeoff from a rough surface, or hitting 其他 objects while flying will significantly change 霍珀's flight path. To compensate for these changes, its 过速装置 charging 速度 in 战斗 has been increased. These changes are a response to feedback that a flying 霍珀 is almost impossible to stop.
  • Updated the «猎人中甲» 底盘
    • 持续时间 of the «干扰器» 状态效果 applied by its 过速装置 is reduced from 18 seconds to 9 seconds.
  • This is due to the updated effect of 干扰器 on 无人机.
  • Updated the 最高装备分数 for 底盘, 炮塔, and 无人机 to 2733 units each.
  • Fixed the bug with 战斗 interface glitches after changing 装备.
  • Fixed the bug with the search bar of the «好友» list.

    • «干扰射击» 装备改造
      • The «干扰器» 状态效果 is applied with every shot, not just the last.
      • The «干扰器» 状态效果’s 持续时间 is reduced from 7 to 5 seconds.

    • «重型等离子炮» 装备改造

      • 炮塔后坐力 is reduced by 80%.
    • This change not only simplifies the use of the 装备改造 on light 底盘, but also significantly reduces the 射程 of 霍珀 in combination with the «轻型结构» 装备改造.
  • 极速炮:
    • «燃烧带» 装备改造
      • Rate of fire is reduced by 25%;
      • 坦克 starts to overheat 75% faster.
  • 雷暴炮:
    • Reload 持续时间 is increased from 3-2.2 to 3.2-2.3 seconds.
    • 暴击伤害半径 is increased to 12 meters.
    • 暴击 hit 几率 is increased from 10% to 15%.
    • The 最高溅射半径 is increased to 2 meters.
    • The percentage of medium 伤害 is reduced to 25%.
    • The percentage of weak 伤害 is reduced to 10%.
    • Impact 启动加速度 is increased from 1.5-3.3 to 2-5.
    • «轻型军械自动装载机» 装备改造
      • 暴击伤害 is reduced by 20%.
    • «穿甲弹药» 装备改造
      • Rate of fire is increased by 15% instead of 10%.
    • «”大锤” rounds» 装备改造
      • 暴击几率 is now 0%.
    • Standard 伤害 now requires more accurate shooting, because its explosion 伤害 is quickly weakened. On the contrary, 暴击伤害 now acts in the entire 半径 of the explosion. According to our idea, such a 雷暴炮 should become less effective when shooting thoughtlessly and more effective when the 玩家 clearly understands when to 射击 accurately, and when to hit the walls and wait for a 暴击 shot.
  • 激光炮:
    • «Electromagnetic accelerator "侦察机"» 装备改造
      • 冲击力 is reduced by 40%.
      • Rate of fire is increased by 20% instead of 30%.
      • Shot warmup time is 30% faster instead of 25%.
    • «大口径弹药» 装备改造
      • Recharge time is increased by 90% instead of 60%.
    • «不稳定轮环» 装备改造
      • 最高暴击几率 is reduced from 70% to 50%.
      • 暴击伤害 is reduced to fixed 50 units.
      • Standard 伤害 is increased by 180%.
    • All these 装备改造 are weakened in different ways due to their 高 efficiency. The most interesting changes came with the «不稳定轮环» 装备改造. Now the main 伤害 dealt is of the standard type, instead of 暴击. This means that this 装备改造 can no longer ignore 激光炮防护 in 战斗, as it was before 暴击伤害 was introduced.
  • 霍珀:
    • 过速装置武器装载时间 is increased from 180 to 210 seconds.
  • 猎人中甲:
    • 过速装置半径 is increased from 25 to 30 meters.
    • The «眩晕» 状态效果’s 持续时间 is increased from 3 to 4 seconds.
    • The «电磁脉冲» 状态效果’s 持续时间 time is increased from 5 to 6 seconds.
  • 十字军:
    • 穿甲 Icicle 伤害 is increased from 1000-2000 to 1500-3000.
      • Reverts the previous 伤害设置 for the 十字军过速装置. They are more justified for slow charging.
  • «助推器» 无人机:
    • 道具 boost is reduced from 20-40% to 15-30%.
    • The performance of this 无人机 is still superior to all 其他无人机.
  • 团队对战 game 模式 is now limited to 150 击杀 in 匹配.
  • The volume of enabling and disabling 道具 has been standardized.
    • The 声音 of the «护甲提升» 道具 will no longer be so loud.
  • The «切尔努什卡» 地图 is available in 匹配 and 专家战场 in 团队对战, 控制点, 互夺军旗, 橄榄球, 突袭, and 团队剑圣模式
  • Added the option to disable the «核能» 道具 in 专家战场设置.

  • Improved the textures of the standard 轰天炮皮肤.
