October 15th (Update 666)

  • Updated 超级礼盒 with the new Mk1 圣骑士底盘 in early access and the newly released 装备改造 for the 特斯拉炮塔 — «震撼闪电»
    • Tired of opponents destroying you? Need to quickly 冰风暴 an enemy? If so, this 装备改造 will 帮助 you greatly. Technology inherited from 猎人中甲's 过速装置 lets the 球 of lightning stop fast-moving opponents for a brief period of time.
  • 激光炮:
    • Shot 炮弹重装时间 (sec) has been decreased from 4,4-2,6 to 3,3-2,6 sec;
    • 冲击力 has been increased from 220-650 to 260-780;
    • 暴击 hit 几率 after dealing crit 伤害 has been increased from 10% to 50%.
  • 镭射炮:
    • Energy per arcade shot (eng) has been decreased from 250 to 0 eng;
    • Sniping shot 炮弹重装时间 has been increased from 3-5 to 10 seconds;
    • 普通 Arcade 伤害 (hp) has been decreased from 335-670 to 290-580 hp;
    • 暴击 Arcade 伤害 (hp) has been decreased from 490-980 to 340-680 hp;
    • 射程 of max 伤害 (m) has been increased from 20-30 to 40-60 m;
    • 射程 of min 伤害 (m) has been increased from 30-40 to 50-70 m;
    • Horizontal 瞄准速度 (deg/sec) has been increased from 15-30 to 20-40 deg/sec.
      • The key change here is that arcade shots no longer consume energy. Earlier, both arcade and sniping shots consumed energy. You could only use the arcade shot if you had enough energy to 射击. Now it’s similar to 特斯拉, where you can still use the arcade 模式 and deal 伤害 to opponents, but at no cost to the energy, even when the 炮塔 is still reloading.
  • 镭射炮’s «重型电容器» 装备改造:
    • Sniping shot 炮弹重装时间 has been increased by 10%.
  • 镭射炮’s «轻型电容器» 装备改造:
    • Sniping shot 炮弹重装时间 has been decreased by 10%.
  • 镭射炮’s «快速射击模式» 装备改造:
    • No longer increases sniping shot 炮弹重装时间.
  • «布鲁特斯» 无人机:
    • Cost of fully upgrading the 无人机 has been decreased from 500 000 to 100 000 水晶.
    • This should make it easier for 玩家 to use the main feature of the 无人机, that is, increasing the strength of the 道具.
  • «驱动器», «骑兵», and «工程师» 无人机:
    • Cost of fully upgrading each 无人机 has been reduced from 1 000 000 to 500 000 水晶.
    • These 无人机 are now at an intermediary 等级 between «布鲁特斯» and higher 等级无人机. They are weaker, but still consume 电池 and enhance the default characteristics of the 坦克.
  • «奔跑者» 无人机:
    • Reduction of 速度提升冷却 has been increased from 5 to 15 seconds.
  • «供应» 无人机:
    • Additional 道具 Active Time has been increased from 5-10 seconds to 5-15 seconds.
  • «助推器» 无人机:
    • 伤害提升 bonus has been decreased from 25%-50% to 20%-40%.
  • «魔术师» 无人机:
    • 速度提升 bonus has been increased from 15%-30% to 20%-40%.
  • The 地图 «群岛匹配» has been removed from the 匹配 pool.

    • It means that 泰坦 and 阿瑞斯 will be as slow as 猛犸象.
    • In the 未来世界, we will make 底盘 of the same class have the same standard 速度, just like we have the same health points number.

September 3rd (Update 661)

Patch Update #661 - Released 3rd September 2021

  • Celebrating 坦克手’ Day;
  • A new kind of 皮肤 is in the game — 蒸汽朋克. During the 坦克手’ Day celebrations you can get these 皮肤 for 离子炮 and 猛犸象, and the animated «Bronze plates» 迷彩, out of the updated 超级礼盒;
  • 火焰炮's default 皮肤 has been updated to an HD version;
  • 特斯拉
    • 最高暴击伤害几率 decreased from 20% to 10%.
    • 拖延协议装备改造:
      • Now decreases lightning 球射程 by 50% instead of 70%
      • Lightning 球炮弹重装时间 increased by 200%:
    • We decided to change the place of this 装备改造 in the game's balance. Decreasing the lighting 球’s 射程 helped to decrease the "kill 动感区域" created by 小组 of 泰坦 but didn't make it harder for them to create such “动感区域”. Increasing the lightning 球’s 炮弹重装时间 will require more teamwork from such 玩家 making it harder for them to create such 动感区域. Also, we’re bringing back the old lighting 球射程 values to retain the idea of long chains. We will keep monitoring the situation.
  • 雷暴炮
    • Ordinary and 暴击伤害 values decreased from 435-880 to 405-810;
    • We’ve decided to decrease the 伤害 of long-射程炮塔 while keeping the number of shots needed to destroy a 坦克 the same;
    • Long 射程炮塔 are very popular nowadays and one of the 原因 why is because of their 伤害. Decreasing 伤害 while keeping the same number of shots to destroy a target should increase the 几率 of a 坦克 surviving after a single shot, if it has been upgraded to even a few MU steps.
  • 激光炮
    • Ordinary 伤害 decreased from 450-900 to 350-700;
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 800-1600 to 655-1310;
  • 马格南
    • Ordinary and 暴击伤害 decreased from 855-1745 to 750-1500;
  • 电磁炮
    • Ordinary 伤害 decreased from 355-705 to 335-670.
    • 暴击伤害 increased from 355-705 to 670-1340.
    • 齐射伤害 decreased from 855-1745 to 750-1500;
  • 镭射炮
    • Ordinary and 最低 sniping 伤害 decreased from 355-705 to 335-670.
    • 暴击伤害 decreased from 500-1000 to 490-980.
    • Charge time in 瞄准模式 increased from 3-3 seconds to 5-3 seconds.
    • «重型电容器» 装备改造 — this 装备改造 now increases 武器装载时间 while in 瞄准模式 by 25% of the default value instead of the previous fixed value of 4 seconds.
    • «轻型电容器» 装备改造 — this 装备改造 now decreases 武器装载时间 while in 瞄准模式 by 50% of the default value instead of the previous fixed value of 2 seconds.
    • In addition to decreasing long 射程炮塔' 伤害, 镭射炮 receives a longer charge time in 瞄准模式 at 低 modifications.
    • These changes to the capacitor 装备改造 won't affect Mk7+ as the time will remain the same - 2 and 4 seconds.
    • Balancing the capacitor 装备改造 was necessary due to 镭射炮’s increased charge time at the lower 等级.
    • 镭射炮 needs a short charge time for dynamic 战斗 at 高等级; however this also makes it too easy at 低等级.
  • Fixed a bug which caused 键盘设置 not to be saved if you changed them while inside a 战斗;
  • Now you need to enter your 双重身份验证 one-time code to disable 双重身份验证.
  • Improvements to the anti-cheat engine.


August 27th (Update 660)

  • 超高 Weekend and updated 超级礼盒;
  • Added 滑膛炮's new «眩晕颗粒» 装备改造. The last shot in the ammo clip 眩晕 every target hit by its 颗粒;
  • 特斯拉's «拖延协议» 装备改造 decreases the 最高 distance of the 球 lightning from 40 metres to 30 metres.
    • The last update has already made it hard to use this 装备改造 with 泰坦. Maybe this change is unnecessary. We will keep an eye on 统计数据.
  • 滑膛炮's «飞龙之息» 装备改造, 轰天炮's «冷冻炮弹» 装备改造 and 激光炮's «冷冻炮弹» 装备改造 no longer decrease 暴击伤害
    • Till this moment we were trying to find the right balance between «着火» and «冷冻» 状态效果. After recent changes it became clear that 冷冻状态效果 needed 特殊 treatment and shouldn't have that huge difference in 伤害 in comparison with 着火状态效果;
  • Anti-cheat improvements.

  • 暴击治疗 is indicated in blue;
  • 暴击 and kill 伤害 indicators are increased in 大小 to differentiate from 普通伤害 indicators.

    • We have started to update the game's interface and 图形 (HTML5 interface, 3D bushes, 超高皮肤). In the 未来世界, we are going to 重制皮肤 one by one for each 炮塔 and 底盘 and make them more modern. There will still only be one default 皮肤 but they will be much better. In order to do this, we have had to choose only one modification 皮肤 for all 炮塔 and 底盘 to 重制 and this is the M3 (Mk7) modification 皮肤. That's a technical requirement and is the first step towards implementing the plan.

        • М2: 20,3 → 17,1;
        • М3: 23,1 → 18,8;
        • М3+: 25 → 20.
      • weak impact percentage increased from 0 to 10%;
      • 锥角 increased from 20° to 25°.
    • «高 pressure pump» alteration for 火焰炮:
      • 锥角 will now decrease by 75% instead of 70%.
    • «高 pressure pump» alteration for 冰风暴:
      • 锥角 will now decrease by 75% instead of 70%.

    • The repairing effect will be interrupted as soon as the 坦克 is fully repaired.

    • Double 伤害
      • 持续时间: 30 seconds
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • 速度提升
      • 持续时间: 30 seconds
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • 地雷
      • 伤害: Unchanged
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%

2011

October 17

  • Amendments made to the «镭射炮» gun.


September 23

  • The incorrect display of «镭射炮» performance in the 车库 has been fixed. All purchased guns have been removed, and the 水晶 paid for them refunded.
  • A new 地图 was added -«Labyrinth» .
  • In the list of tips that appear when loading a game, a new recommendation— «Do not talk.»


September 22

  • 镭射炮 gun re-balancing was finished. Previous version of the gun was confiscated from all 玩家 who bought it and spent 水晶 were repaid.
  • In new version of the gun we:
    • simplified 控制;
    • added possibility to 射击 without using 辽源;
    • added possibility to stay in sniper 模式 as long as you want with fully charged gun;
    • removed black filling in 辽源模式;
    • visually enhanced the 辽源;
    • changed 箱子 and 旗子 displaying in 辽源模式, now they become semitransparent to simplify 瞄准.
    • Four new 迷彩 added to the 车库: Irbis, Jade, Lead, Needle
    • added new 地图公路大战 from MonkeyMagic.


September 9

  • We have added «Registration» button to first 战斗 interface. Now new 玩家 can register, not finishing the first 战斗. User still can achieve the first 等级 and get 奖励 for this during the first fight or in any 其他战斗.
  • 密码 length was limited to 32 symbols.


September 1

  • Payments for 水晶 using Paypal have resumed.
  • The cost of all payments through SMS are now include VAT.
  • The 最低 payment through SMS payment for MTC subscribers has been set at 300 roubles. This change was made by the service provider itself. In the past an error could be experienced when attempting to make a payment less than 300 roubles.
  • The ability to make a one symbol 密码 without an 电子邮件 has been excluded.


August 25

  • The registration form has been improved. It has become smaller, more convenient — nicer.
  • 战斗 creation has been optimized for newbies, thanks to that fact in such 战斗 there will be more 玩家.
  • In the loading screen «TV grid» has been replaced with the game logo.


August 18

  • We have changed the formula of user rating calculating. Now it doesn’t count 水晶 bought for real money. The rating of all users will be recalculated in two days.
  • We have simplified the game entering mechanics. Now after clicking the Start

button a newcomer enters the 战斗 without registration. There he can meet 坦克手 of 新兵, 二等兵 and 一等兵等级. Such a 玩家 automatically gets the 昵称 RecruitNNNNN, where NNNNN is unique number.

  • A 玩家 is offered to fill the registration form only after

reaching 二等兵等级.

  • If you are not a newcomer, but also found yourself in a 战斗 with newbies and with 昵称 RecruitNNNNN, then click «I have an 账号» button in the upper part of the game menu. We have created a basic achievement system, which 帮助 newcomers to learn some basic elements of the game. Now you get 水晶 prizes for such actions, as registration after the first 战斗, joining the first 战斗 after registration, first buying in the 车库 etc.
  • We have changed loading indications. Now it looks like the charging

mechanism of artillery gun. Also game advices are shown during loading.

  • We have simplified the registration form.
  • The Tab button now is functional in all fields.
  • You need to enter less information to register. Only 昵称 and

密码 are required.

  • The Hall of Fame button was removed from the game menu.
  • Every 玩家 now can create a no-道具战斗 without a 通行证. The

创建者 also can enter this 战斗 without a 通行证.

  • We have improved the WebMoney payment option. Now you can choose the

currency and amount of 水晶 right in the payment section.

  • The 镭射炮 gun became visually shorter.
  • We have created a 特殊迷彩 for moderators.
  • 玩家 notification regarding the Double 水晶 bonus card was

optimized.

  • If a 玩家 has such a card, he sees an alternative version of the 购买

button.

  • The sum on the Add button in the 车库 is adjusted for Double

水晶.

  • Notification about an active Double 水晶 bonus card is shown in

the payment section.

  • The PayPal button is temporary removed from the payment section. We’ll start to

take PayPal payments again soon.

  • Now you can’t skip the nick checking procedure.
  • The respawn was fixed in the blue 团队 on 山顶城堡地图.
  • The wall bug was fixed on 辽源地图.
  • The 迷彩 «Champion» (for 军团 Tournament winners) and Acid (for TOF

winners) were given 防护 against the 镭射炮.

  • Now you can’t 射击 from under the bridge right through the slope of

the bridge.

  • We have finished work on the German version of 3D坦克. Get ready to meet German

玩家 soon!

March 23

  • New registration form.


March 21

  • We have realized sources storage in local SharedObject of Flash 玩家. It 允许 us to abandon browser caching system, which is not very reliable. For example, sources could disappear from browser cache because of its limited 大小. Now sources are downloaded from the 服务器 only if they were changed. It can drastically reduce time of game loading.

  • 离子炮 is experimentally strengthened for one week. You can discuss the current 统计 and post your impressions/suggestions here
  • The referral banned display problem is now solved.
2009

December 31

  • It’s the New Year’s eve, and all the guns have gone crazy!


December, 30

  • Fixed an issue with 磁力炮’s 治疗 action. Previously, 治疗 was done in percent and not in HP.
  • Added an option to enable/disable the 战斗聊天. If the combat 聊天 is turned off, messages will not be displayed. However, you may press enter to view all the messages you missed as well as to write one yourself.


December 29

  • Changed aggregator of payment terminals. Now we receive payments through terminals in four countries
  • Redesigned section for 水晶 purchasing
  • Improved ban system
  • Added new SMS-payment aggregator. Now we receive payments in 67 countries

  • Fixed bug with automatic naming of 战斗 creation
  • Changed #plans, #faq и #rules considering new 论坛
  • Improved 阴影 under buildings on the snow
  • Links to new 论坛 are automatically changed into clickable ones
  • Changed tree-旗子 design


December 23

  • Winter came to all the 地图
  • 旗子 were temporarily turned into fir-trees
  • Introduced system of automatic change of capital letters into lowercase ones
  • Fixed bug of damaging through walls with the 帮助 of 火焰炮
  • The principle of 暂停模式 has been changed. The 暂停模式 is activated by pressing P or 暂停 button. If a 坦克 has been destroyed while 暂停 is active, the 坦克 doesn’t spawn until the 暂停模式 is disabled. In the beginning of a new round all 坦克 are spawned regardless of active 暂停.
  • In 聊天 when entering #plans appears conversion into clickable link to the corresponding 论坛 thread. in 聊天 #plans is displayed as Задачи и планы разработчиков in Russian localization and Developers’ 任务 and plans in English one
  • 地图城堡争夺 and 黑色城堡 were temporarily disconnected to be prepared for winter


December 18

  • In 聊天 when entering #faq or #rules appears conversion into clickable link to the corresponding 论坛 thread. In 聊天 #faq is displayed as FAQ for Russian and English localization, and #rules is displayed as Правила in Russian localization and Rules in the English one
  • In 聊天 the links to the 论坛 are clickable
  • Own 坦克 doesn’t have now nick and 等级 indication next to health/charge indication stripes
  • Fixed bug of single-use items use of a 坦克 in inactive (translucent) 模式
  • Fixed bug of First Aid single use when having full health
  • Added new 地图: 十字路口 from eras, 混乱城市 from DJ_Efreitor, 城堡争夺 from GrUm, 黑色城堡 from GrUm, 山城大战 from DJ_Efreitor.

August 7

  • Added 聊天 orders to 禁止 messages from users:
    • /禁止 name – 禁止 messages from the 玩家 (works in 大厅 and 战斗聊天).
    • /unblock name – resume messages from 玩家 (works in 大厅 and 战斗聊天).
    • /blocklist – view the list of blocked 玩家 (works in 大厅).
    • /unblockall – clear the list of blocked 玩家 (works in 大厅).

The list of blocked users is kept in Shared Objects, so if you enter the game from the 其他 computer – it won't work.
